TYPE: game.Game
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the main ludeme that describes the players, mode, equipment and rules of a game.
NEW CTOR
(game <string> <players> [<mode>] <equipment> <rules>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the game.
PARAM JAVADOC: <players>: The players of the game.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<mode>]: The mode of the game [Alternating].
PARAM JAVADOC: <equipment>: The equipment of the game.
PARAM JAVADOC: <rules>: The rules of the game.
EXAMPLE: (game "Tic-Tac-Toe" (players 2) (equipment { (board (square 3)) (piece "Disc" P1) (piece "Cross" P2) }) (rules (play (move Add (to (sites Empty)))) (end (if (is Line 3) (result Mover Win))) ) )
TYPE: game.equipment.Equipment
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the equipment list of the game.
NEW CTOR
(equipment {<item>})
PARAM JAVADOC: {<item>}: The items (container, component etc.).
EXAMPLE: (equipment { (board (square 3)) (piece "Disc" P1) (piece "Cross" P2) })
REMARKS: To define the items (container, component etc.) of the game. Any type of component or container described in this chapter may be used as an <item> type.
TYPE: game.equipment.Item
TYPE JAVADOC: Provides a Grammar placeholder for items to go in the equipment collection.

TYPE: game.equipment.component.Card
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a card with specific properties such as the suit or the rank of the  card in the deck.
NEW CTOR
(card <string> <roleType> <cardType> rank:int value:int trumpRank:int trumpValue:int suit:int [<moves>] [maxState:int] [maxCount:int] [maxValue:int])
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the card.
PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The owner of the card.
PARAM JAVADOC: <cardType>: The type of a card chosen from the possibilities in the CardType ludeme.
PARAM JAVADOC: rank:int: The rank of the card in the deck.
PARAM JAVADOC: value:int: The value of the card.
PARAM JAVADOC: trumpRank:int: The trump rank of the card in the deck.
PARAM JAVADOC: trumpValue:int: The trump value of the card.
PARAM JAVADOC: suit:int: The suit of the card.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<moves>]: The moves associated with the component.
PARAM JAVADOC: [maxState:int]: To set the maximum local state the game should check.
PARAM JAVADOC: [maxCount:int]: To set the maximum count the game should check.
PARAM JAVADOC: [maxValue:int]: To set the maximum value the game should check.
EXAMPLE: (card "Card" Shared King rank:6 value:4 trumpRank:3 trumpValue:4 suit:1)
REMARKS: This ludeme creates a specific card. If this ludeme is used with no deck defined, the generated card will be not included in a deck by default. See also Deck ludeme.
TYPE: game.equipment.component.Component
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a component.
TYPE: game.equipment.component.Die
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a single non-stochastic die used as a piece.
NEW CTOR
(die <string> <roleType> numFaces:int [<directionFacing>] [<moves>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the die.
PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The owner of the die.
PARAM JAVADOC: numFaces:int: The number of faces of the die.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<directionFacing>]: The direction of the component.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<moves>]: The moves associated with the component.
EXAMPLE: (die "Die6" All numFaces:6)
REMARKS: The die defined with this ludeme will be not included in a dice container and cannot be rolled with the roll ludeme, but can be turned to show each of its faces.
TYPE: game.equipment.component.Piece
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a piece.
NEW CTOR
(piece <string> [<roleType>] [<directionFacing>] [<flips>] [<moves>] [maxState:int] [maxCount:int] [maxValue:int])
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the piece.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The owner of the piece [Each].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<directionFacing>]: The direction of the piece.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<flips>]: The corresponding values to flip, e.g. (flip 1 2) 1 is flipped to 2 and 2 is flipped to 1.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<moves>]: The moves associated with the piece.
PARAM JAVADOC: [maxState:int]: To set the maximum local state the game should check.
PARAM JAVADOC: [maxCount:int]: To set the maximum count the game should check.
PARAM JAVADOC: [maxValue:int]: To set the maximum value the game should check.
EXAMPLE: (piece "Pawn" Each)
EXAMPLE: (piece "Disc" Neutral (flips 1 2))
EXAMPLE: (piece "Dog" P1 (step (to if:(is Empty (to)))))
REMARKS: Useful to create a pawn, a disc or a representation of an animal for example.
TYPE: game.equipment.component.tile.Domino
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a single domino.
NEW CTOR
(domino <string> <roleType> value:int value2:int [<moves>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the domino.
PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The owner of the domino.
PARAM JAVADOC: value:int: The first value of the domino.
PARAM JAVADOC: value2:int: The second value of the domino.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<moves>]: The moves associated with the component.
EXAMPLE: (domino "Domino45" Shared value:4 value2:5)
REMARKS: The domino defined with this ludeme will be not included in the dominoes container by default and so cannot be shuffled with other dominoes.
TYPE: game.equipment.component.tile.Path
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the internal path of a tile component.
NEW CTOR
(path from:int [slotsFrom:int] to:int [slotsTo:int] colour:int)
PARAM JAVADOC: from:int: The "from" side of the connection.
PARAM JAVADOC: [slotsFrom:int]: The slot of the "from" side [0].
PARAM JAVADOC: to:int: The "to" side of the connection.
PARAM JAVADOC: [slotsTo:int]: The slot of the "to" side [0].
PARAM JAVADOC: colour:int: The colour of the connection.
EXAMPLE: (path from:0 to:2 colour:1)
REMARKS: To define the path of the internal connection of a tile component. The number side 0 = the first direction of the tiling, in general 0 = North.
TYPE: game.equipment.component.tile.Tile
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a tile, a component following the tiling with internal connection.
NEW CTOR
(tile <string> [<roleType>] ([{<stepType>}]  | [{{<stepType>}}]) [numSides:int] ([slots:{int}]  | [slotsPerSide:int]) [{<path>}] [<flips>] [<moves>] [maxState:int] [maxCount:int] [maxValue:int])
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the tile.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The owner of the tile.
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<stepType>}]: A turtle graphics walk to define the shape of a large tile.
PARAM JAVADOC: [{{<stepType>}}]: Many turtle graphics walks to define the shape of a large tile.
PARAM JAVADOC: [numSides:int]: The number of sides of the tile.
PARAM JAVADOC: [slots:{int}]: The number of slots for each side.
PARAM JAVADOC: [slotsPerSide:int]: The number of slots for each side if this is the same number for each side [1].
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<path>}]: The connection in the tile.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<flips>]: The corresponding values to flip, e.g. (flip 1 2) 1 is flipped to 2 and 2 is flipped to 1.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<moves>]: The associated moves of this component.
PARAM JAVADOC: [maxState:int]: To set the maximum local state the game should check.
PARAM JAVADOC: [maxCount:int]: To set the maximum count the game should check.
PARAM JAVADOC: [maxValue:int]: To set the maximum value the game should check.
EXAMPLE: (tile "TileX" numSides:4 { (path from:0 to:2 colour:1) (path from:1 to:3 colour:2) } )
TYPE: game.equipment.container.Container
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a container.
SUBCLASS: game.equipment.container.board.Board

SUBCLASS: game.equipment.container.board.custom.SurakartaBoard

TYPE: game.equipment.container.board.Board
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a board by its graph, consisting of vertex locations and edge pairs.
NEW CTOR
(board <graphFunction> ([<track>]  | [{<track>}]) ([<values>] ([{<values>}]) [use:<siteType>] [largeStack:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph function used to build the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<track>]: The track on the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<track>}]: The tracks on the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<values>]: The range values of a graph element used for deduction puzzle.
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<values>}]: The range values of many graph elements used for deduction puzzle.
PARAM JAVADOC: [use:<siteType>]: Graph element type to use by default [Cell].
PARAM JAVADOC: [largeStack:<boolean>]: The game can involves stack(s) higher than 32.
EXAMPLE: (board (graph vertices:{ {1 0} {2 0} {0 1} {1 1} {2 1} {3 1} {0 2} {1 2} {2 2} {3 2} {1 3} {2 3}} edges:{ {0 2} {0 3} {3 2} {3 4} {1 4} {4 5} {1 5} {3 7} {4 8} {6 7} {7 8} {8 9} {6 10} {11 9} {10 7} {11 8}} ) )
REMARKS: The values range are used for deduction puzzles. The state model for these puzzles is a Constraint Satisfaction Problem (CSP) model, possibly with a variable for each graph element (i.e. vertex, edge and cell), each with a range of possible values.
TYPE: game.equipment.container.board.Boardless
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a boardless container growing in function of the pieces played.
NEW CTOR
(boardless <tilingBoardlessType> [<dimFunction>] [largeStack:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <tilingBoardlessType>: The tiling of the boardless container.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<dimFunction>]: The "fake" size of the board used for boardless [41].
PARAM JAVADOC: [largeStack:<boolean>]: The game can involves stack(s) higher than 32.
EXAMPLE: (boardless Hexagonal)
REMARKS: The playable sites of the board will be all the sites adjacent to the places already played/placed. No pregeneration is computed on the graph except the centre.
TYPE: game.equipment.container.board.Track
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a named track for a container, which is typically the board.
NEW CTOR
(track <string> ({int}  | <string>  | {<trackStep>}) [loop:<boolean>] ([int]  | [<roleType>]) [directed:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the track.
PARAM JAVADOC: {int}: List of integers describing board site indices.
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: Description including site indices and cardinal.
PARAM JAVADOC: {<trackStep>}: Description using track steps. directions (N, E, S, W).
PARAM JAVADOC: [loop:<boolean>]: True if the track is a loop [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [int]: The owner of the track [0].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The role of the owner of the track [Neutral].
PARAM JAVADOC: [directed:<boolean>]: True if the track is directed [False].
EXAMPLE: (track "Track" "1,E,N,W" loop:True)
EXAMPLE: (track "Track1" {6 12..7 5..0 13..18 20..25 End} P1 directed:True)
EXAMPLE: (track "Track1" "20,3,W,N1,E,End" P1 directed:True)
REMARKS: Tracks are typically used for race games, or any game in which pieces move around a track. A number after a direction indicates the number of steps in that direction. For example, "N1,E3" means that track goes North for one step then turns East for three steps.
TYPE: game.equipment.container.board.custom.MancalaBoard
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a Mancala-style board.
NEW CTOR
(mancalaBoard int int [store:<storeType>] [numStores:int] [largeStack:<boolean>] ([<track>]  | [{<track>}]))
PARAM JAVADOC: int: The number of rows.
PARAM JAVADOC: int: The number of columns.
PARAM JAVADOC: [store:<storeType>]: The type of the store.
PARAM JAVADOC: [numStores:int]: The number of store.
PARAM JAVADOC: [largeStack:<boolean>]: The game can involves stack(s) higher than 32.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<track>]: The track on the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<track>}]: The tracks on the board.
EXAMPLE: (mancalaBoard 2 6)
TYPE: game.equipment.container.board.custom.SurakartaBoard
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a Surakarta-style board.
NEW CTOR
(surakartaBoard <graphFunction> [loops:int] [from:int] [largeStack:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph function used to build the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [loops:int]: Number of loops, i.e. special capture tracks [(minDim - 1) / 2].
PARAM JAVADOC: [from:int]: Which row to start loops from [1].
PARAM JAVADOC: [largeStack:<boolean>]: The game can involves stack(s) higher than 32.
EXAMPLE: (surakartaBoard (square 6) loops:2)
REMARKS: Surakata-style boards have loops that pieces must travel around in order to capture other pieces. The following board shapes are supported: Square, Rectangle, Hexagon, Triangle.
TYPE: game.equipment.container.other.Deck
TYPE JAVADOC: Generates a deck of cards.
NEW CTOR
(deck [<roleType>] [cardsBySuit:int] [suits:int] [{<card>}])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The owner of the deck [Shared].
PARAM JAVADOC: [cardsBySuit:int]: The number of cards per suit [13].
PARAM JAVADOC: [suits:int]: The number of suits in the deck [4].
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<card>}]: Specific data about each kind of card for each suit.
EXAMPLE: (deck)
EXAMPLE: (deck { (card Seven rank:0 value:0 trumpRank:0 trumpValue:0) (card Eight rank:1 value:0 trumpRank:1 trumpValue:0) (card Nine rank:2 value:0 trumpRank:6 trumpValue:14) (card Ten rank:3 value:10 trumpRank:4 trumpValue:10) (card Jack rank:4 value:2 trumpRank:7 trumpValue:20) (card Queen rank:5 value:3 trumpRank:2 trumpValue:3) (card King rank:6 value:4 trumpRank:3 trumpValue:4) (card Ace rank:7 value:11 trumpRank:5 trumpValue:11) })
TYPE: game.equipment.container.other.Dice
TYPE JAVADOC: Generates a set of dice.
NEW CTOR
(dice [d:int] ([faces:{int}]  | [facesByDie:{{int}}]  | [from:int]) [<roleType>] num:int [biased:{int}])
PARAM JAVADOC: [d:int]: The number of faces of the die [6].
PARAM JAVADOC: [faces:{int}]: The values of each face.
PARAM JAVADOC: [facesByDie:{{int}}]: The values of each face for each die.
PARAM JAVADOC: [from:int]: The starting value of each die [1].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The owner of the dice [Shared].
PARAM JAVADOC: num:int: The number of dice in the set.
PARAM JAVADOC: [biased:{int}]: The biased values of each die.
EXAMPLE: (dice d:2 from:0 num:4)
REMARKS: Used for any dice game to define a set of dice. Only the set of dice can be rolled.

TYPE: game.equipment.other.Hints

PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: The name of these hints.
PARAM JAVADOC: {<hint>}: The different hints.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The graph element type of the sites.

REMARKS: Used for any deduction puzzle with hints.
TYPE: game.equipment.other.Map

PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: The name of the map ["Map"].
PARAM JAVADOC: {<pair>}: The pairs of each map.
EXAMPLE: (map "Entry" { (pair P1 "D1") (pair P2 "E8") (pair P3 "H4") (pair P4 "A5")})
EXAMPLE: (map { (pair 5 19) (pair 7 9) (pair 34 48) (pair 36 38) } )
EXAMPLE: (map {(pair P1 P4) (pair P2 P5) (pair P3 P6) (pair P4 P1) (pair P5 P2) (pair P6 P3)})

PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: The name of the map ["Map"].

PARAM JAVADOC: {<int>}: The values of the map.
EXAMPLE: (map {1..9} {1 2 4 8 16 32 64 128 256})
REMARKS: Used to map a site to another or to map an integer to another.
TYPE: game.equipment.other.Regions
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a static region on the board.

PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The owner of the region [P1].

PARAM JAVADOC: {<regionTypeStatic>}: Pre-computed static regions corresponding to this region.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: Name of this hint region (for deduction puzzles).
EXAMPLE: (regions P1 { (sites Side NE) (sites Side SW) } )
EXAMPLE: (regions "Replay" {14 24 43 53})
EXAMPLE: (regions "Traps" (sites {"C3" "C6" "F3" "F6"}))
TYPE: game.functions.booleans.ToBool
TYPE JAVADOC: Converts a IntFunction or a FloatFunction to a boolean (false if 0, else  true).
NEW CTOR
(toBool (<int>  | <floatFunction>))
PARAM JAVADOC: <int>: The int function.
PARAM JAVADOC: <floatFunction>: The float function.
EXAMPLE: (toBool (count Moves))
EXAMPLE: (toBool (sqrt 2))
TYPE: game.functions.booleans.all.All
TYPE JAVADOC: Returns whether all aspects of the specified query are true.
NEW CTOR
(all Groups [<siteType>] [<direction>] [of:<boolean>] If:<boolean>)
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The type of the graph elements of the group.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<direction>]: The directions of the connection between elements in the group [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [of:<boolean>]: The condition on the pieces to include in the group [(= (to) (mover))].
PARAM JAVADOC: If:<boolean>: The condition for each group to verify.
EXAMPLE: (all Groups if:(= 3 (count Sites in:(sites))))
NEW CTOR
(all Values <intArrayFunction> If:<boolean>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <intArrayFunction>: The array to check.
PARAM JAVADOC: If:<boolean>: The condition to check.
EXAMPLE: (all Values (values Remembered) if:(> 2 (value)))
NEW CTOR
(all <allSitesType> <region> If:<boolean>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <allSitesType>: The query type to perform.
PARAM JAVADOC: <region>: The region to check.
PARAM JAVADOC: If:<boolean>: The condition to check.
EXAMPLE: (all Sites (sites Occupied by:Mover) if:(= 2 (size Stack at:(site))))
NEW CTOR
(all <allSimpleType>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <allSimpleType>: The query type to perform.
EXAMPLE: (all DiceUsed)
EXAMPLE: (all Passed)
EXAMPLE: (all DiceEqual)
TYPE: game.functions.booleans.all.AllSimpleType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the query types that can be used for an {\tt (all ...)} test with no parameter.
CONST JAVADOC: DiceUsed: Returns whether all the dice have been used in the current turn.
CONST JAVADOC: DiceEqual: Returns whether all the dice are equal when they are rolled.
CONST JAVADOC: Passed: Returns whether all players have passed in succession.
TYPE: game.functions.booleans.all.AllSitesType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the query types that can be used for an {\tt (all ...)} test related to sites.
CONST JAVADOC: Sites: Returns whether all the sites satisfy a condition.
CONST JAVADOC: Different: Returns whether all the sites are different.

TYPE JAVADOC: Returns whether a given property can be achieved in the current game state.
NEW CTOR
(can Move <moves>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <moves>: List of moves.
EXAMPLE: (can Move (forEach Piece))
TYPE: game.functions.booleans.deductionPuzzle.ForAll
TYPE JAVADOC: Returns true if the constraint is satisfied for each element.
NEW CTOR
(forAll <puzzleElementType> <boolean>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <puzzleElementType>: The type of the graph element.
PARAM JAVADOC: <boolean>: The constraint to check.
EXAMPLE: (forAll Hint (is Count (sites Around (from) includeSelf:True) of:1 (hint) ) )
REMARKS: This is used to test a constraint on each vertex, edge, face or site with a hint. This works only for deduction puzzles.
TYPE: game.functions.booleans.deductionPuzzle.all.All
TYPE JAVADOC: Whether the specified query is all true for a deduction puzzle.
NEW CTOR
(all Different [<siteType>] [<region>] ([except:<int>]  | [excepts:{<int>}]))
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: Type of graph elements to return [Cell].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<region>]: The region to check [Regions].
PARAM JAVADOC: [except:<int>]: The exception on the test.
PARAM JAVADOC: [excepts:{<int>}]: The exceptions on the test.
EXAMPLE: (all Different)
EXAMPLE: (all Different except:0)
TYPE: game.functions.booleans.deductionPuzzle.is.Is
TYPE JAVADOC: Whether the specified query is true for a deduction puzzle.
NEW CTOR
(is Solved)
EXAMPLE: (is Solved)
NEW CTOR
(is Unique [<siteType>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The graph element type [Cell].
EXAMPLE: (is Unique)
NEW CTOR
(is <isPuzzleRegionResultType> [<siteType>] [<region>] [of:<int>] [<string>] <int>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <isPuzzleRegionResultType>: The query type to perform.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The graph element of the region [Default SiteType of the board].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<region>]: The region [Regions].
PARAM JAVADOC: [of:<int>]: The index of the piece [1].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: The name of the region to check.
PARAM JAVADOC: <int>: The result to check.
EXAMPLE: (is Count (sites All) of:1 8)
EXAMPLE: (is Sum 5)
TYPE: game.functions.booleans.deductionPuzzle.is.IsPuzzleRegionResultType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the types of Is test for puzzle according to region and a specific result to check.
CONST JAVADOC: Count: To check if the count of a region is equal to the result.
CONST JAVADOC: Sum: To check if the sum of a region is equal to the result.
TYPE: game.functions.booleans.is.Is
TYPE JAVADOC: Returns whether the specified query about the game state is true or not.
NEW CTOR
(is <isAngleType> [<siteType>] at:<int> <boolean> <boolean>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <isAngleType>: The type of query to perform.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The graph element type [default of the board].
PARAM JAVADOC: at:<int>: The site to look the angle.
PARAM JAVADOC: <boolean>: The condition on the left site.
PARAM JAVADOC: <boolean>: The condition on the right site.
EXAMPLE: (is Acute at:(last To) (is Enemy (who at:(site))) (is Enemy (who at:(site))))
NEW CTOR
(is Hidden [<hiddenData>] [<siteType>] at:<int> [level:<int>] (to:<player>  | To:<roleType>))
PARAM JAVADOC: [<hiddenData>]: The type of hidden data [Invisible].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The graph element type [default of the board].
PARAM JAVADOC: at:<int>: The site to set the hidden information.
PARAM JAVADOC: [level:<int>]: The level to set the hidden information [0].
PARAM JAVADOC: to:<player>: The player with these hidden information.
PARAM JAVADOC: To:<roleType>: The roleType with these hidden information.
EXAMPLE: (is Hidden at:(to) to:Mover)
NEW CTOR
(is Repeat [<repetitionType>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<repetitionType>]: The type of repetition [Positional].
EXAMPLE: (is Repeat Positional)
NEW CTOR
(is Pattern {<stepType>} [<siteType>] [from:<int>] ([what:<int>]  | [whats:{<int>}]))
PARAM JAVADOC: {<stepType>}: The walk describing the pattern.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The type of the site from to detect the pattern.
PARAM JAVADOC: [from:<int>]: The site from to detect the pattern [(last To)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [what:<int>]: The piece to check in the pattern [piece in from].
PARAM JAVADOC: [whats:{<int>}]: The sequence of pieces to check in the pattern [piece in from].
EXAMPLE: (is Pattern {F R F R F})
NEW CTOR
(is <isTreeType> (<player>  | <roleType>))

(is <isConnectType> [<int>] [<siteType>] [at:<int>] [<direction>] ({<region>}  | <roleType>  | <regionTypeStatic>))
PARAM JAVADOC: <isConnectType>: The type of query to perform.

NEW CTOR
(is Line [<siteType>] <int> [<absoluteDirection>] ([through:<int>]  | [throughAny:<region>]) ([<roleType>] ([what:<int>]  | [whats:{<int>}]) [exact:<boolean>] [contiguous:<boolean>] [If:<boolean>] [byLevel:<boolean>] [top:<boolean>] [throughHowMuch:<int>] [isVisible:<boolean>] [useOpposites:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The graph element type [default SiteType of the board].
PARAM JAVADOC: <int>: Minimum length of lines.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<absoluteDirection>]: Direction category to which potential lines must belong [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [through:<int>]: Location through which the line must pass.
PARAM JAVADOC: [throughAny:<region>]: The line must pass through at least one of these sites.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The owner of the pieces making a line [Mover].
PARAM JAVADOC: [what:<int>]: The index of the component composing the line [(mover)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [whats:{<int>}]: The indices of the components composing the line.
PARAM JAVADOC: [exact:<boolean>]: If true, then lines cannot exceed minimum length [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [contiguous:<boolean>]: If true, the line has to be contiguous [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: [If:<boolean>]: The condition on each site on the line [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: [byLevel:<boolean>]: If true, then lines are detected in using the level in a stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [top:<boolean>]: If true, then lines are detected in using only the top level in a stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [throughHowMuch:<int>]: The number of minimum component types to compose the line
PARAM JAVADOC: [isVisible:<boolean>]: If a line has to be visible from above (and not cut by other components) (used in 3D games)
PARAM JAVADOC: [useOpposites:<boolean>]: Whether to use the opposite radial to try and find line (i.e whether to iterate in both opposite directions of analyzed component to find line)
EXAMPLE: (is Line 3)
EXAMPLE: (is Line 5 Orthogonal if:(not (is In (to) (sites Mover))))
NEW CTOR
(is Loop [<siteType>] ([surround:<roleType>]  | [{<roleType>}]) [<direction>] [<int>] ([<int>]  | [<region>]) [path:<boolean>])

PARAM JAVADOC: [surround:<roleType>]: Used to define the inside condition of the loop.
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<roleType>}]: The list of items inside the loop.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<direction>]: The direction of the connection [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<int>]: The owner of the looping pieces [Mover].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<int>]: The starting point of the loop [(last To)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<region>]: The region to start to detect the loop.
PARAM JAVADOC: [path:<boolean>]: Whether to detect loops in the paths of pieces (e.g. Trax).
EXAMPLE: (is Loop)
EXAMPLE: (is Loop (mover) path:True)

PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The role of the player owning the pieces on the path.
PARAM JAVADOC: length:<rangeFunction>: The range size of the path.
PARAM JAVADOC: [closed:<boolean>]: Is used to detect closed components [False].

TYPE: game.functions.booleans.math.And

NEW CTOR
(and <boolean> <boolean>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <boolean>: First condition.
PARAM JAVADOC: <boolean>: Second condition.
EXAMPLE: (and (= (who at:(last To)) (mover)) (!= (who at:(last From)) (mover)))
NEW CTOR
(and {<boolean>})
PARAM JAVADOC: {<boolean>}: The list of conditions to check.
EXAMPLE: (and {(= (who at:(last To)) (mover)) (!= (who at:(last From)) (mover)) (is Pending)})
REMARKS: This test returns false as soon as any of its conditions return false, so it pays to test conditions that are faster and more likely to fail first.

TYPE: game.functions.graph.generators.basis.square.DiagonalsType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines how to handle diagonal relations on the Square tiling.
CONST JAVADOC: Implied: Diagonal connections (not edges) between opposite corners.
CONST JAVADOC: Solid: Solid edges between opposite diagonals, which split the square into four triangles.
CONST JAVADOC: SolidNoSplit: Solid edges between opposite diagonals, but do not split the square into four triangles.
CONST JAVADOC: Alternating: Every second diagonal is a solid edge, as per Alquerque boards.
CONST JAVADOC: Concentric: Concentric diagonal rings from the centre.
CONST JAVADOC: Radiating: Diagonals radiating from the centre.

TYPE: game.functions.graph.generators.basis.tiling.TilingType

CONST JAVADOC: T3464: Rhombitrihexahedral tiling (e.g. Kensington).

CONST JAVADOC: T33344: Semi-regular tiling made up of alternating rows of squares and triangles.
CONST JAVADOC: T3636: Semi-regular tiling made up of triangles and hexagons.
CONST JAVADOC: T4612: Semi-regular tiling made up of squares, hexagons and dodecagons.
CONST JAVADOC: T333333_33434: Tiling 3.3.3.3.3.3,3.3.4.3.4.

TYPE: game.functions.graph.generators.shape.concentric.Concentric
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a board based on a tiling of concentric shapes.
NEW CTOR
(concentric (<concentricShapeType>  | sides:<dimFunction>  | {<dimFunction>}) [rings:<dimFunction>] [steps:<dimFunction>] [midpoints:<boolean>] [joinMidpoints:<boolean>] [joinCorners:<boolean>] [stagger:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <concentricShapeType>: Shape of board rings.
PARAM JAVADOC: sides:<dimFunction>: Number of sides (for polygonal shapes).
PARAM JAVADOC: {<dimFunction>}: Number of cells per circular ring.
PARAM JAVADOC: [rings:<dimFunction>]: Number of rings [3].
PARAM JAVADOC: [steps:<dimFunction>]: Number of steps for target boards with multiple sites per ring [null].
PARAM JAVADOC: [midpoints:<boolean>]: Whether to add vertices at edge midpoints [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: [joinMidpoints:<boolean>]: Whether to join concentric midpoints [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: [joinCorners:<boolean>]: Whether to join concentric corners [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [stagger:<boolean>]: Whether to stagger cells in concentric circular rings [False].
EXAMPLE: (concentric Square rings:3)
EXAMPLE: (concentric Triangle rings:3 joinMidpoints:False joinCorners:True)
EXAMPLE: (concentric Hexagon rings:3 joinMidpoints:False joinCorners:True)
EXAMPLE: (concentric sides:5 rings:3)
EXAMPLE: (concentric { 8 })
EXAMPLE: (concentric { 0 8 })
EXAMPLE: (concentric { 1 4 8 } stagger:True)
EXAMPLE: (concentric Target rings:4)
EXAMPLE: (concentric Target rings:4 steps:16)
REMARKS: Morris or Merels boards are examples of square concentric boards. Circular tilings are centred around a ``pivot'' point. For circular boards defined by a list of cell counts, the first count should be 0 (centre point) or 1 (centre cell).
TYPE: game.functions.graph.generators.shape.concentric.ConcentricShapeType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines star shape types for known board types.
CONST JAVADOC: Square: Concentric squares rings, e.g. Morris boards.
CONST JAVADOC: Triangle: Concentric triangles.
CONST JAVADOC: Hexagon: Concentric hexagons.
CONST JAVADOC: Target: Concentric circles, like a target.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Add
TYPE JAVADOC: Adds elements to a graph.
NEW CTOR
(add [<graphFunction>] [vertices:{{<floatFunction>}}] ([edges:{{{<floatFunction>}}}]  | [Edges:{{<dimFunction>}}]) [edgesCurved:{{{<floatFunction>}}}] ([cells:{{{<floatFunction>}}}]  | [Cells:{{<dimFunction>}}]) [connect:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<graphFunction>]: The graph to remove elements from.
PARAM JAVADOC: [vertices:{{<floatFunction>}}]: Locations of vertices to add.
PARAM JAVADOC: [edges:{{{<floatFunction>}}}]: Locations of end points of edges to add.
PARAM JAVADOC: [Edges:{{<dimFunction>}}]: Indices of end point vertices to add.
PARAM JAVADOC: [edgesCurved:{{{<floatFunction>}}}]: Locations of end points and tangents of edges to add.
PARAM JAVADOC: [cells:{{{<floatFunction>}}}]: Locations of vertices of faces to add.
PARAM JAVADOC: [Cells:{{<dimFunction>}}]: Indices of vertices of faces to add.
PARAM JAVADOC: [connect:<boolean>]: Whether to connect newly added vertices to nearby neighbours [False].
EXAMPLE: (add (square 4) vertices:{ {1 2} })
EXAMPLE: (add edges:{ {{0 0} {1 1}} })
EXAMPLE: (add (square 4) cells:{ {{1 1} {1 2} {3 2} {3 1}} })
EXAMPLE: (add (square 2) edgesCurved:{ {{0 0} {1 0} {1 2} {-1 2}} })
REMARKS: The elements to be added can be vertices, edges or faces. Edges and faces will create the specified vertices if they don't already exist. When defining curved edges, the first and second set of numbers are the end points locations and the third and fourth set of numbers are the tangent directions for the edge end points.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Clip
TYPE JAVADOC: Returns the result of clipping a graph to a specified shape.
NEW CTOR
(clip <graphFunction> <poly>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: Graph to clip.
PARAM JAVADOC: <poly>: Float points defining clip region.
EXAMPLE: (clip (square 4) (poly { { 1 1 } { 1 3 } { 4 0 } }))
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Complete
TYPE JAVADOC: Creates an edge between each pair of vertices in the graph.
NEW CTOR
(complete <graphFunction> [eachCell:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph to complete.
PARAM JAVADOC: [eachCell:<boolean>]: Whether to complete each cell individually.
EXAMPLE: (complete (hex 1))
EXAMPLE: (complete (hex 3) eachCell:True)
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Dual
TYPE JAVADOC: Returns the weak dual of the specified graph.
NEW CTOR
(dual <graphFunction>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph to take the weak dual of.
EXAMPLE: (dual (square 5))
REMARKS: The weak dual of a graph is obtained by creating a vertex at the midpoint of each face, then connecting with an edge vertices corresponding to adjacent faces. This is equivalent to the dual of the graph without the single ``outside'' vertex. The weak dual is non-transitive and always produces a smaller graph; applying (dual (dual <graph>)) does not restore the original graph.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Hole
TYPE JAVADOC: Cuts a hole in a graph according to a specified shape.
NEW CTOR
(hole <graphFunction> <poly>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: Graph to clip.
PARAM JAVADOC: <poly>: Float points defining hole region.
EXAMPLE: (hole (square 8) (poly { { 2.5 2.5 } { 2.5 5.5 } { 4.5 5.5 } { 4.5 4.5 } {5.5 4.5 } { 5.5 2.5 } }))
REMARKS: Any face of the graph whose midpoint falls within the hole is removed, as are any edges or vertices isolated as a result.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Intersect
TYPE JAVADOC: Returns the intersection of two or more graphs.
NEW CTOR
(intersect <graphFunction> <graphFunction>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: First graph to intersect.
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: Second graph to intersect.
EXAMPLE: (intersect (square 4) (rectangle 2 5))
NEW CTOR
(intersect {<graphFunction>})
PARAM JAVADOC: {<graphFunction>}: Graphs to intersect.
EXAMPLE: (intersect { (rectangle 6 2) (square 4) (rectangle 7 2) })
REMARKS: The intersection of two or more graphs is composed of the vertices and edges that occur in all of those graphs.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Keep

(keep <graphFunction> <poly>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: Graph to modify.
PARAM JAVADOC: <poly>: Float points defining keep region.
EXAMPLE: (keep (square 4) (poly { { 1 1 } { 1 3 } { 4 0 } }))
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Layers
TYPE JAVADOC: Makes multiple layers of the specified graph for 3D games.
NEW CTOR
(layers <dimFunction> <graphFunction>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <dimFunction>: Number of layers.
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph to layer.
EXAMPLE: (layers 3 (square 3)))
REMARKS: The layers are stacked upon each one 1 unit apart. Layers will be shown in isometric view from the side in a future version.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.MakeFaces

(makeFaces <graphFunction>)

TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Merge
TYPE JAVADOC: Returns the result of merging two or more graphs.
NEW CTOR
(merge <graphFunction> <graphFunction> [connect:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: First graph to merge.
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: Second graph to merge.
PARAM JAVADOC: [connect:<boolean>]: Whether to connect newly added vertices to nearby neighbours [False].
EXAMPLE: (merge (rectangle 6 2) (rectangle 3 5))
NEW CTOR
(merge {<graphFunction>} [connect:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: {<graphFunction>}: Graphs to merge.
PARAM JAVADOC: [connect:<boolean>]: Whether to connect newly added vertices to nearby neighbours [False].
EXAMPLE: (merge { (rectangle 6 2) (square 4) (rectangle 7 2) })
REMARKS: The graphs are overlaid with each other, such that incident vertices (i.e. those with the same location) are merged into a single vertex.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Recoordinate
TYPE JAVADOC: Regenerates the coordinate labels for the elements of a graph.
NEW CTOR
(recoordinate [<siteType>] [<siteType>] [<siteType>] <graphFunction>)
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: First site type to recoordinate (Vertex/Edge/Cell).
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: Second site type to recoordinate (Vertex/Edge/Cell).
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: Third site type to recoordinate (Vertex/Edge/Cell).
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph whose vertices are to be renumbered.
EXAMPLE: (recoordinate (merge (rectangle 2 5) (square 5)))
EXAMPLE: (recoordinate Vertex (merge (rectangle 2 5) (square 5)))
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Remove
TYPE JAVADOC: Removes elements from a graph.
NEW CTOR
(remove <graphFunction> ([cells:{{{<float>}}}]  | [Cells:{<dimFunction>}]) ([edges:{{{<float>}}}] ([Edges:{{<dimFunction>}}]) ([vertices:{{<float>}}] ([Vertices:{<dimFunction>}]) [trimEdges:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph to remove elements from.
PARAM JAVADOC: [cells:{{{<float>}}}]: Locations of vertices of faces to remove.
PARAM JAVADOC: [Cells:{<dimFunction>}]: Indices of faces to remove.
PARAM JAVADOC: [edges:{{{<float>}}}]: Locations of end points of edges to remove.
PARAM JAVADOC: [Edges:{{<dimFunction>}}]: Indices of end points of edges to remove.
PARAM JAVADOC: [vertices:{{<float>}}]: Locations of vertices to remove.
PARAM JAVADOC: [Vertices:{<dimFunction>}]: Indices of vertices to remove.
PARAM JAVADOC: [trimEdges:<boolean>]: Whether to trim edges orphaned by removing faces [True].
EXAMPLE: (remove (square 4) vertices:{ { 0.0 3.0 } { 0.5 2 } })
EXAMPLE: (remove (square 4) cells:{ 0 1 2 } edges:{ {0 1} {1 2} } vertices:{ 1 4 })
NEW CTOR
(remove <graphFunction> <poly> [trimEdges:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: Graph to clip.
PARAM JAVADOC: <poly>: Float points defining hole region.
PARAM JAVADOC: [trimEdges:<boolean>]: Whether to trim edges orphaned by removing faces [True].
EXAMPLE: (remove (square 8) (poly { { 2.5 2.5 } { 2.5 5.5 } { 4.5 5.5 } { 4.5 4.5 } {5.5 4.5 } { 5.5 2.5 } }))
REMARKS: The elements to be removed can be vertices, edges or faces. Elements whose vertices can't be found will be ignored. Be careful when removing by index, as the graph is modified and renumbered with each removal. It is recommended to specify indices in decreasing order and to avoid removing vertices, edges and/or faces by index on the same call (instead, you can chain multiple removals by index together, one for each element type).
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Renumber
TYPE JAVADOC: Renumbers the vertices of a graph into sequential order.
NEW CTOR
(renumber [<siteType>] [<siteType>] [<siteType>] <graphFunction>)
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: First site type to renumber (Vertex/Edge/Cell).
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: Second site type to renumber (Vertex/Edge/Cell).
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: Third site type to renumber (Vertex/Edge/Cell).
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph whose vertices are to be renumbered.
EXAMPLE: (renumber (merge (rectangle 2 5) (square 5)))
EXAMPLE: (renumber Vertex (merge (rectangle 2 5) (square 5)))
REMARKS: Vertices are renumbered from the lower left rightwards and upwards, in an upwards reading order. Renumbering can be useful after a union or merge operation combines different graphs.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Rotate
TYPE JAVADOC: Rotates a graph by the specified number of degrees anticlockwise.
NEW CTOR
(rotate <floatFunction> <graphFunction>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <floatFunction>: Number of degrees to rotate anticlockwise.
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph to rotate.
EXAMPLE: (rotate 45 (square 5))
REMARKS: The vertices within the graph are rotated about the graph's midpoint.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Scale
TYPE JAVADOC: Scales a graph by the specified amount.
NEW CTOR
(scale <floatFunction> [<floatFunction>] [<floatFunction>] <graphFunction>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <floatFunction>: Amount to scale in the x direction.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<floatFunction>]: Amount to scale in the y direction [scaleX].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<floatFunction>]: Amount to scale in the z direction [1].
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph to scale.
EXAMPLE: (scale 2 (square 5))
EXAMPLE: (scale 2 3.5 (square 5))
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Shift

NEW CTOR

PARAM JAVADOC: <floatFunction>: Amount to translate in the x direction.
PARAM JAVADOC: <floatFunction>: Amount to translate in the y direction.

PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph to rotate.

TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Subdivide
TYPE JAVADOC: Subdivides graph cells about their midpoint.

PARAM JAVADOC: [min:<dimFunction>]: Minimum cell size to subdivide [1].
EXAMPLE: (subdivide (tiling T3464 2) min:6)
REMARKS: Each cell with N sides, where N > min, will be split into N cells.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Trim
TYPE JAVADOC: Trims orphan vertices and edges from a graph.
NEW CTOR
(trim <graphFunction>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: The graph to be trimmed.
EXAMPLE: (trim (dual (square 5)))
REMARKS: An orphan vertex is a vertex with no incident edge (note that pivot vertices are not removed). An orphan edge is an edge with an end point that has no incident edges apart from the edge itself.
TYPE: game.functions.graph.operators.Union
TYPE JAVADOC: Returns the union of two or more graphs.
NEW CTOR
(union <graphFunction> <graphFunction> [connect:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: First graph to combine.
PARAM JAVADOC: <graphFunction>: Second graph to combine.
PARAM JAVADOC: [connect:<boolean>]: Whether to connect newly added vertices to nearby neighbours [False].
EXAMPLE: (union (square 5) (square 3))
NEW CTOR
(union {<graphFunction>} [connect:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: {<graphFunction>}: Graphs to merge.
PARAM JAVADOC: [connect:<boolean>]: Whether to connect newly added vertices to nearby neighbours [False].
EXAMPLE: (union { (rectangle 6 2) (square 4) (rectangle 7 2) })
REMARKS: The graphs are simply combined with each other, with no connection between them.

PARAM JAVADOC: [<relationType>]: The relation type of the steps [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<step>]: Define a particular step move to step.
PARAM JAVADOC: [newRotation:<int>]: Define a new rotation at each step move in using the (value) iterator for the rotation.
PARAM JAVADOC: <int>: The first site.
PARAM JAVADOC: <int>: The second site.
PARAM JAVADOC: <region>: The second region.
EXAMPLE: (count Steps (where (id "King")) (where (id "Queen")))
NEW CTOR
(count StepsOnTrack ([<roleType>]  | [<player>]  | [<string>]) [<int>] [<int>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The role of the owner of the track [Mover].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<player>]: The owner of the track [(mover)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: The name of the track.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<int>]: The first site.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<int>]: The second site.
EXAMPLE: (count StepsOnTrack (last From) (last To))

(nextPhase ([<roleType>]  | [<player>]) [<boolean>] [<string>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The roleType of the player [Shared].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<player>]: The index of the player.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<boolean>]: The condition to satisfy to go to another phase [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: The name of the phase.
EXAMPLE: (nextPhase Mover (= (count Moves) 10) "Movement")
REMARKS: If no phase is specified, moves to the next phase in the list, wrapping back to the first phase if needed. The ludeme returns Undefined (-1) if the condition is false or if the named phase does not exist.
TYPE: game.rules.phase.Phase
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the phase of a game.
NEW CTOR
(phase <string> [<roleType>] [<mode>] <play> [<end>] ([<nextPhase>]  | [{<nextPhase>}]))
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the phase.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The roleType of the owner of the phase [Shared].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<mode>]: The mode of this phase within the game [mode defined for whole game)].
PARAM JAVADOC: <play>: The playing rules of this phase.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<end>]: The ending rules of this phase.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<nextPhase>]: The next phase of this phase.
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<nextPhase>}]: The next phases of this phase.
EXAMPLE: (phase "Movement" (play (forEach Piece)))
REMARKS: A phase can be defined for only one player.
TYPE: game.rules.play.Play
TYPE JAVADOC: Checks the playing rules of the game.
NEW CTOR
(play <moves>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <moves>: The legal moves of the playing rules.
EXAMPLE: (play (forEach Piece))

TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.decision.Decision
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines moves that involve a decision by the player.
SUBCLASS: game.rules.play.moves.decision.Move
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.decision.Move
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a decision move.
NEW CTOR
(move Swap Players (<int>  | <roleType>) (<int> (<roleType>) [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <int>: The index of the first player.
PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The role of the first player.
PARAM JAVADOC: <int>: The index of the second player.
PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The role of the second player.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Swap Players P1 P2)
NEW CTOR
(move Swap Pieces [<int>] [<int>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<int>]: The first location [(lastFrom)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<int>]: The second location [(lastTo)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Swap Pieces (last To) (last From))
NEW CTOR
(move Remove [<siteType>] (<int>  | <region>) [level:<int>] [at:<whenType>] [count:<int>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The graph element type of the location [Cell (or Vertex if the main board uses this)].
PARAM JAVADOC: <int>: The location to remove a piece.
PARAM JAVADOC: <region>: The locations to remove a piece.
PARAM JAVADOC: [level:<int>]: The level to remove a piece [top level].
PARAM JAVADOC: [at:<whenType>]: When to perform the removal [immediately].
PARAM JAVADOC: [count:<int>]: The number of pieces to remove [1].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Remove (last To))
NEW CTOR
(move Set TrumpSuit (<int>  | <difference>) [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <int>: The suit to choose.
PARAM JAVADOC: <difference>: The possible suits to choose.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Set TrumpSuit (card Suit at:(handSite Shared)))
NEW CTOR
(move Set NextPlayer (<player>  | <intArrayFunction>) [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <player>: The data of the next player.
PARAM JAVADOC: <intArrayFunction>: The indices of the next players.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Set NextPlayer (player (mover)))
NEW CTOR
(move Set Rotation [<to>] ([{<int>}]  | [<int>]) [previous:<boolean>] [next:<boolean>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<to>]: Description of the ``to'' location [(to (from))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<int>}]: The index of the possible new directions.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<int>]: The index of the possible new direction.
PARAM JAVADOC: [previous:<boolean>]: True to allow movement to the left [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: [next:<boolean>]: True to allow movement to the right [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Set Rotation)
EXAMPLE: (move Set Rotation (to (last To)) next:False)
NEW CTOR
(move Step [<from>] [<direction>] <to> [stack:<boolean>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: Description of ``from'' location [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<direction>]: The directions of the move [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: Description of the ``to'' location.
PARAM JAVADOC: [stack:<boolean>]: True if the move is applied to a stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: Moves to apply after this one.
EXAMPLE: (move Step (to if:(is Empty (to))) )
EXAMPLE: (move Step Forward (to if:(is Empty (to))) )
EXAMPLE: (move Step (directions {FR FL}) (to if:(or (is Empty (to)) (is Enemy (who at:(to)))) (apply (remove (to)))) )
NEW CTOR
(move Slide [<from>] [<string>] [<direction>] [<between>] [<to>] [stack:<boolean>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: Description of the ``from'' location [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: The track on which to slide.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<direction>]: The directions of the move [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<between>]: Description of the location(s) between ``from'' and ``to''.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<to>]: Description of the ``to'' location.
PARAM JAVADOC: [stack:<boolean>]: True if the move is applied to a stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: Moves to apply after this one.
EXAMPLE: (move Slide)
EXAMPLE: (move Slide Orthogonal)
EXAMPLE: (move Slide "AllTracks" (between if:(or (= (between) (from)) (is In (between) (sites Empty)) ) ) (to if:(is Enemy (who at:(to))) (apply (remove (to))) ) (then (set Counter)) )
NEW CTOR
(move Shoot <piece> [<from>] [<absoluteDirection>] [<between>] [<to>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <piece>: The data about the piece to shoot.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: The ``from'' location [(lastTo)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<absoluteDirection>]: The direction to follow [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<between>]: The location(s) between ``from'' and ``to''.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<to>]: The condition on the ``to'' location to allow shooting [(to if:(in (to) (sites Empty)))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Shoot (piece "Dot0"))
NEW CTOR
(move Select <from> [<to>] [<roleType>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <from>: Describes the ``from'' location to select [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<to>]: Describes the ``to'' location to select.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The mover of the move.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Select (from) (then (remove (last To))))
EXAMPLE: (move Select (from (sites Occupied by:Mover) if:(!= (state at:(to)) 0) ) (to (sites Occupied by:Next) if:(!= (state at:(to)) 0) ) (then (set State at:(last To) (% (+ (state at:(last From)) (state at:(last To))) 5) ) ) )
NEW CTOR
(move <moveMessageType> (<string>  | {<string>}) [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <moveMessageType>: The type of move.
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The message.
PARAM JAVADOC: {<string>}: The messages.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Propose "End")
EXAMPLE: (move Vote "End")
NEW CTOR
(move Promote [<siteType>] [<int>] <piece> ([<player>]  | [<roleType>]) [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The graph element type [default SiteType of the board].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<int>]: The location of the piece to promote [(to)].
PARAM JAVADOC: <piece>: The data about the promoted pieces.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<player>]: Data of the owner of the promoted piece.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: RoleType of the owner of the promoted piece.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Promote (last To) (piece {"Queen" "Knight" "Bishop" "Rook"}) Mover)
NEW CTOR
(move <moveSimpleType> [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <moveSimpleType>: The type of move.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Pass)
NEW CTOR
(move Leap [<from>] {{<stepType>}} [forward:<boolean>] [rotations:<boolean>] <to> [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: The from location [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: {{<stepType>}}: The walk to follow.
PARAM JAVADOC: [forward:<boolean>]: True if the move can only move forward according to the direction of the piece [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [rotations:<boolean>]: True if the move includes all the rotations of the walk [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: The data about the location to move.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Leap { {F F R F} {F F L F} } (to if:(or (is Empty (to)) (is Enemy (who at:(to)))) (apply (if (is Enemy (who at:(to))) (remove (to) ) ) ) ) )
NEW CTOR
(move Hop [<from>] [<direction>] [<between>] <to> [stack:<boolean>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: The data of the from location [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<direction>]: The directions of the move [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<between>]: The information about the locations between ``from'' and ``to'' [(between if:True)].
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: The condition on the location to move.
PARAM JAVADOC: [stack:<boolean>]: True if the move has to be applied for stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Hop (between if:(is Enemy (who at:(between))) (apply (remove (between))) ) (to if:(is Empty (to))) )
EXAMPLE: (move Hop Orthogonal (between if:(is Friend (who at:(between))) (apply (remove (between))) ) (to if:(is Empty (to))) )
NEW CTOR
(move <from> <to> [count:<int>] [copy:<boolean>] [stack:<boolean>] [<roleType>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <from>: The data of the ``from'' location [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: The data of the ``to'' location.
PARAM JAVADOC: [count:<int>]: The number of pieces to move.
PARAM JAVADOC: [copy:<boolean>]: Whether to duplicate the piece rather than moving it [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [stack:<boolean>]: To move a complete stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The mover of the move.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move (from (last To)) (to (last From)))
EXAMPLE: (move (from (handSite Mover)) (to (sites Empty)))
EXAMPLE: (move (from (to)) (to (sites Empty)) count:(count at:(to)))
EXAMPLE: (move (from (handSite Shared)) (to (sites Empty)) copy:True )
NEW CTOR
(move Bet (<player>  | <roleType>) <rangeFunction> [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <player>: The data about the player to bet.
PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The RoleType of the player to bet.
PARAM JAVADOC: <rangeFunction>: The range of the bet.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Bet P1 (range 0 5))
NEW CTOR
(move <moveSiteType> [<piece>] <to> [count:<int>] [stack:<boolean>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <moveSiteType>: The type of move.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<piece>]: The data about the components to add.
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: The data on the location to add.
PARAM JAVADOC: [count:<int>]: The number of components to add [1].
PARAM JAVADOC: [stack:<boolean>]: True if the move has to be applied on a stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (move Add (to (sites Empty)))
EXAMPLE: (move Claim (to Cell (site)))

TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Add
TYPE JAVADOC: Places one or more component(s) at a collection of sites or at one specific  site.
NEW CTOR
(add [<piece>] <to> [count:<int>] [stack:<boolean>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<piece>]: The data about the components to add.
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: The data on the location to add.
PARAM JAVADOC: [count:<int>]: The number of components to add [1].
PARAM JAVADOC: [stack:<boolean>]: True if the move has to be applied on a stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (add (to (sites Empty)))
EXAMPLE: (add (to Cell (sites Empty Cell)))
EXAMPLE: (add (piece "Disc0") (to (last From)))
EXAMPLE: (add (piece "Disc0") (to (sites Empty)) (then (attract)) )
REMARKS: The ``to'' location is not updated until the move is made.
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Apply

EXAMPLE: (apply if:(is Mover P1))
NEW CTOR
(apply <nonDecision>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <nonDecision>: The moves to apply to make the effect.
EXAMPLE: (apply (moveAgain))
NEW CTOR
(apply If:<boolean> <nonDecision>)
PARAM JAVADOC: If:<boolean>: The condition to satisfy to get the effect moves.
PARAM JAVADOC: <nonDecision>: The moves to apply to make the effect.
EXAMPLE: (apply if:(is Mover P1) (moveAgain))

TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Claim
TYPE JAVADOC: Claims a site by adding a piece of the specified colour there.
NEW CTOR
(claim [<piece>] <to> [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<piece>]: The data about the components to claim.
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: The data on the location to claim.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (claim (to Cell (site)) (then (and (addScore Mover 1) (moveAgain))))
REMARKS: This ludeme is used for graph games.
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Custodial
TYPE JAVADOC: Is used to apply an effect to all the sites flanked between two sites.
NEW CTOR
(custodial [<from>] [<absoluteDirection>] [<between>] [<to>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: The data about the sites used as an origin to flank [(from (last To))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<absoluteDirection>]: The direction to compute the flanking [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<between>]: The condition and effect on the pieces flanked [(between if:(is Enemy (between)) (apply (remove (between))))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<to>]: The condition on the pieces surrounding [(to if:(is Friend (to)))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (custodial (from (last To)) Orthogonal (between (max 1) if:(is Enemy (who at:(between))) (apply (remove (between))) ) (to if:(is Friend (who at:(to)))) )
REMARKS: Used for example in all the Tafl games.
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Deal
TYPE JAVADOC: Deals cards or dominoes to each player.
NEW CTOR
(deal <dealableType> [<int>] [beginWith:<int>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <dealableType>: Type of deal.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<int>]: The number of components to deal [1].
PARAM JAVADOC: [beginWith:<int>]: To start to deal with a specific player.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (deal Cards 3 beginWith:(mover))
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Directional
TYPE JAVADOC: Is used to apply an effect to all the pieces in a direction from a location.
NEW CTOR
(directional [<from>] [<direction>] [<to>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: The origin of the move [(from (last To))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<direction>]: The directions to use [(directions from:(last From) to:(last To))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<to>]: The condition of the location to apply the effect [(to if:(is Enemy (to)) (apply (remove (from))))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (directional (from (last To)) (to if:(is Enemy (who at:(to))) (apply (remove (to))) ))
REMARKS: For example, used in Fanorona.

TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Enclose
TYPE JAVADOC: Applies a move to an enclosed group.
NEW CTOR
(enclose [<siteType>] [<from>] [<direction>] [<between>] [numException:<int>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The graph element type [default site type of the board].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: The origin of the enclosed group [(from (last To))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<direction>]: The direction to use [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<between>]: The condition and effect on the pieces enclosed [(between if:(is Enemy (between)) (apply (remove (between))))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [numException:<int>]: The number of liberties allowed in the group to enclose [0].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (enclose (from (last To)) Orthogonal (between if:(is Enemy (who at:(between))) (apply (remove (between) ) ) ))
REMARKS: A group of components is 'enclosed' if it has no adjacent empty sites, where board sides count as boundaries. This ludeme is used for surround capture games such as Go.

TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.FromTo
TYPE JAVADOC: Moves a piece from one site to another, possibly in another container, with  no direction link between the ``from'' and ``to'' sites.
NEW CTOR
(fromTo <from> <to> [count:<int>] [copy:<boolean>] [stack:<boolean>] [<roleType>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <from>: The data of the ``from'' location [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: The data of the ``to'' location.
PARAM JAVADOC: [count:<int>]: The number of pieces to move.
PARAM JAVADOC: [copy:<boolean>]: Whether to duplicate the piece rather than moving it [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [stack:<boolean>]: To move a complete stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<roleType>]: The mover of the move.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (fromTo (from (last To)) (to (last From)))
EXAMPLE: (fromTo (from (handSite Mover)) (to (sites Empty)))
EXAMPLE: (fromTo (from (to)) (to (sites Empty)) count:(count at:(to)))
EXAMPLE: (fromTo (from (handSite Shared)) (to (sites Empty)) copy:True )
REMARKS: If the ``copy'' parameter is set, then a copy of the piece is duplicated at the ``to'' site rather than actually moving there.
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Hop
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a hop in which a piece hops over a hurdle (the {\it pivot}) in a direction.
NEW CTOR
(hop [<from>] [<direction>] [<between>] <to> [stack:<boolean>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: The data of the from location [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<direction>]: The directions of the move [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<between>]: The information about the locations between ``from'' and ``to'' [(between if:true)].
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: The condition on the location to move.
PARAM JAVADOC: [stack:<boolean>]: True if the move has to be applied for stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (hop (between if:(is Enemy (who at:(between))) (apply (remove (between))) ) (to if:(is Empty (to))) )
EXAMPLE: (hop Orthogonal (between if:(is Friend (who at:(between))) (apply (remove (between))) ) (to if:(is Empty (to))) )
REMARKS: Capture moves in Draughts are typical hop moves. Note that we extend the standard definition of ``hop'' to include cases where the pivot is empty, for example in games such as Lines of Action and Quantum Leap.
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Intervene

(intervene [<from>] [<absoluteDirection>] [<between>] [<to>] [<then>])

TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Leap
TYPE JAVADOC: Allows a player to leap a piece to sites defined by walks through the board graph.
NEW CTOR
(leap [<from>] {{<stepType>}} [forward:<boolean>] [rotations:<boolean>] <to> [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: The site to leap from [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: {{<stepType>}}: The walk that defines the landing site(s).
PARAM JAVADOC: [forward:<boolean>]: Whether to only keep moves that land forwards [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [rotations:<boolean>]: Whether to apply the leap to all rotations [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: Details about the site to move to.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: Moves to apply after the leap.
EXAMPLE: (leap { {F F R F} {F F L F} } (to if:(or (is Empty (to)) (is Enemy (who at:(to)))) (apply (if (is Enemy (who at:(to))) (remove (to) ) ) ) ) )
REMARKS: Use this ludeme to make leaping moves to pre-defined destination sites that do not care about intervening pieces, such as knight moves in Chess.

TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Select
TYPE JAVADOC: Selects either a site or a pair of ``from'' and ``to'' locations.

REMARKS: This ludeme is used to select one or two sites in order to apply a consequence to them. If the ``to'' location is not specified, then it is assumed to be the same as the 'from' location.
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Shoot

TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Slide
TYPE JAVADOC: Slides a piece in a direction through a number of sites.
NEW CTOR
(slide [<from>] [<string>] [<direction>] [<between>] [<to>] [stack:<boolean>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: Description of the ``from'' location [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: The track on which to slide.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<direction>]: The directions of the move [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<between>]: Description of the location(s) between ``from'' and ``to''.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<to>]: Description of the ``to'' location.
PARAM JAVADOC: [stack:<boolean>]: True if the move is applied to a stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: Moves to apply after this one.
EXAMPLE: (slide)
EXAMPLE: (slide Orthogonal)
EXAMPLE: (slide "AllTracks" (between if:(or (= (between) (from)) (is In (between) (sites Empty)) ) ) (to if:(is Enemy (who at:(to))) (apply (remove (to))) ) (then (set Counter)) )
REMARKS: The rook in Chess is an example of a piece that slides in Orthogonal directions. Pieces can be constrained to slide along predefined tracks, e.g. see Surakarta. Note that we extend the standard definition of ``slide'' to allow pieces to slide through other pieces if a specific condition is given, but that pieces are assumed to slide through empty sites only by default.
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Sow
TYPE JAVADOC: Sows counters by removing them from a site then placing them one-by-one at  each consecutive site along a track.
NEW CTOR
(sow [<siteType>] [<int>] [count:<int>] [numPerHole:<int>] [<string>] [owner:<int>] [If:<boolean>] [sowEffect:<moves>] [apply:<nonDecision>] [includeSelf:<boolean>] [origin:<boolean>] [skipIf:<boolean>] ([backtracking:<boolean>]  | [forward:<boolean>]) [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The graph element type [default SiteType of the board].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<int>]: The origin of the sowing [(lastTo)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [count:<int>]: The number of pieces to sow [(count (lastTo))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [numPerHole:<int>]: The number of pieces to sow in each hole [1].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: The name of the track to sow [The first track if it exists].
PARAM JAVADOC: [owner:<int>]: The owner of the track.
PARAM JAVADOC: [If:<boolean>]: The condition to capture some counters after sowing [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: [sowEffect:<moves>]: The effect to apply to each hole sowed.
PARAM JAVADOC: [apply:<nonDecision>]: The move to apply if the condition is satisfied.
PARAM JAVADOC: [includeSelf:<boolean>]: True if the origin is included in the sowing [True].
PARAM JAVADOC: [origin:<boolean>]: True to place a counter in the origin at the start of sowing [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [skipIf:<boolean>]: The condition to skip a hole during the sowing.
PARAM JAVADOC: [backtracking:<boolean>]: Whether to apply the capture backwards from the ``to'' site.
PARAM JAVADOC: [forward:<boolean>]: Whether to apply the capture forwards from the ``to'' site.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (sow if:(and (is In (to) (sites Next)) (or (= (count at:(to)) 2) (= (count at:(to)) 3)) ) apply:(fromTo (from (to)) (to (mapEntry (mover))) count:(count at:(to))) includeSelf:False backtracking:True)
REMARKS: Sowing is used in Mancala games. A track must be defined on the board in order for sowing to work.
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Step
TYPE JAVADOC: Moves to a connected site.
NEW CTOR
(step [<from>] [<direction>] <to> [stack:<boolean>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<from>]: Description of ``from'' location [(from)].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<direction>]: The directions of the move [Adjacent].
PARAM JAVADOC: <to>: Description of the ``to'' location.
PARAM JAVADOC: [stack:<boolean>]: True if the move is applied to a stack [False].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: Moves to apply after this one.
EXAMPLE: (step (to if:(is Empty (to))) )
EXAMPLE: (step Forward (to if:(is Empty (to))) )
EXAMPLE: (step (directions {FR FL}) (to if:(or (is Empty (to)) (is Enemy (who at:(to)))) (apply (remove (to)))) )
REMARKS: The (to ...) parameter is used to specify a condition on the site to step and on the effect to apply. But the region function in entry of that parameter is ignored because the region to move is implied by a step move.
TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.Surround
TYPE JAVADOC: Is used to apply an effect to all the sites surrounded in a specific  direction.

PARAM JAVADOC: [<between>]: The condition and effect on the pieces to surround [(between if:(is Enemy (to)) (apply (remove (to))))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [<to>]: The condition on the pieces surrounding [(to if:(isFriend (between)))].
PARAM JAVADOC: [except:<int>]: The number of exceptions allowed to apply the effect [0].

TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.requirement.Do
TYPE JAVADOC: Applies two moves in order, according to given conditions.
NEW CTOR
(do <moves> [next:<moves>] [ifAfterwards:<boolean>] [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <moves>: Moves to be applied first.
PARAM JAVADOC: [next:<moves>]: Follow-up moves computed after the first set of moves. The prior moves are not returned if that set of moves is empty.
PARAM JAVADOC: [ifAfterwards:<boolean>]: Moves must satisfy this condition afterwards to be legal.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (do (roll) next:(if (!= (count Pips) 0) (forEach Piece)))
EXAMPLE: (do (fromTo (from (sites Occupied by:All container:(mover))) (to (sites LineOfPlay))) ifAfterwards:(is PipsMatch) )
REMARKS: Use ifAfterwards to filter out moves that do not satisfy some required condition after they are applied.

TYPE: game.rules.play.moves.nonDecision.effect.requirement.Priority

PARAM JAVADOC: {<moves>}: The list of moves.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (priority { (forEach Piece "Leopard" (step (to if:(is Enemy (who at:(to)))))) (forEach Piece "Leopard" (step (to if:(is In (to) (sites Empty))))) })
NEW CTOR
(priority <moves> <moves> [<then>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <moves>: The first set of moves.
PARAM JAVADOC: <moves>: The second set of moves.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (priority (forEach Piece "Leopard" (step (to if:(is Enemy (who at:(to)))))) (forEach Piece "Leopard" (step (to if:(is In (to) (sites Empty)))) ))
REMARKS: To prioritise a list of legal moves over another. For example in some draughts games, if you can capture, you must capture, if not you can move normally.

TYPE JAVADOC: Iterates over a set of items.

PARAM JAVADOC: [<siteType>]: The type of the graph elements of the group [default SiteType of the board].

PARAM JAVADOC: <moves>: The moves to apply.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<then>]: The moves applied after that move is applied.
EXAMPLE: (forEach Die (if (= (pips) 5) (or (forEach Piece "Pawn") (forEach Piece "King_noCross")) (if (= (pips) 4) (forEach Piece "Elephant") (if (= (pips) 3) (forEach Piece "Knight") (if (= (pips) 2) (forEach Piece "Boat") ) ) ) ) )

(forEach Value min:<int> max:<int> <startRule>)
PARAM JAVADOC: min:<int>: The minimal value.
PARAM JAVADOC: max:<int>: The maximal value.
PARAM JAVADOC: <startRule>: The starting rule to apply.
EXAMPLE: (forEach Value min:1 max:5 (set Hidden What at:10 level:(value) to:P1))
NEW CTOR
(forEach Player <startRule>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <startRule>: The starting rule to apply.
EXAMPLE: (forEach Player (set Hidden What at:1 to:Player))
NEW CTOR
(forEach <intArrayFunction> <startRule>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <intArrayFunction>: The list of players.
PARAM JAVADOC: <startRule>: The starting rule to apply.
EXAMPLE: (forEach (players Ally of:(next)) (set Hidden What at:1 to:Player))
TYPE: game.rules.start.place.Place

NEW CTOR

PARAM JAVADOC: [<string>]: The name of the container.

TYPE: game.types.board.BasisType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines known tiling types for boards.
CONST JAVADOC: NoBasis: No tiling; custom graph.
CONST JAVADOC: Triangular: Triangular tiling.
CONST JAVADOC: Square: Square tiling.
CONST JAVADOC: Hexagonal: Hexagonal tiling.
CONST JAVADOC: T33336: Semi-regular tiling made up of hexagons surrounded by triangles.
CONST JAVADOC: T33344: Semi-regular tiling made up of alternating rows of squares and triangles.
CONST JAVADOC: T33434: Semi-regular tiling made up of squares and pairs of triangles.
CONST JAVADOC: T3464: Rhombitrihexahedral tiling (e.g. Kensington).
CONST JAVADOC: T3636: Semi-regular tiling 3.6.3.6 made up of hexagons with interstitial triangles.
CONST JAVADOC: T4612: Semi-regular tiling made up of squares, hexagons and dodecagons.
CONST JAVADOC: T488: Semi-regular tiling 4.8.8. made up of octagons with interstitial squares.
CONST JAVADOC: T31212: Semi-regular tiling made up of triangles and dodecagons.
CONST JAVADOC: T333333_33434: Tiling 3.3.3.3.3.3,3.3.4.3.4.
CONST JAVADOC: SquarePyramidal: Square pyramidal tiling (e.g. Shibumi).
CONST JAVADOC: HexagonalPyramidal: Hexagonal pyramidal tiling.
CONST JAVADOC: Concentric: Concentric tiling (e.g. Morris boards, wheel boards, ...).
CONST JAVADOC: Circle: Circular tiling (e.g. Round Merels).
CONST JAVADOC: Spiral: Spiral tiling (e.g. Mehen).
CONST JAVADOC: Dual: Tiling derived from the weak dual of a graph.
CONST JAVADOC: Brick: Brick tiling using 1x2 rectangular brick tiles.
CONST JAVADOC: Mesh: Mesh formed by random spread of points within an outline shape.
CONST JAVADOC: Morris: Morris tiling with concentric square rings and empty centre.
CONST JAVADOC: Celtic: Tiling on a square grid based on Celtic knotwork.
CONST JAVADOC: QuadHex: Quadhex board consisting of a hexagon tessellated by quadrilaterals (e.g. Three Player Chess).

TYPE: game.util.moves.Between
TYPE JAVADOC: Gets all the conditions or effects related to the location between ``from'' and ``to''.
NEW CTOR
(between [before:<int>] [<rangeFunction>] [after:<int>] [If:<boolean>] [trail:<int>] [<apply>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [before:<int>]: Lead distance up to ``between'' section.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<rangeFunction>]: Range of the ``between'' section.
PARAM JAVADOC: [after:<int>]: Trailing distance after ``between'' section.
PARAM JAVADOC: [If:<boolean>]: The condition on the location.
PARAM JAVADOC: [trail:<int>]: The piece to let on the location.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<apply>]: Actions to apply.
EXAMPLE: (between if:(is Enemy (who at:(between))) (apply (remove (between))) )

TYPE: metadata.ai.Ai
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines metadata that can help AIs in the Ludii app to play this game at a  stronger level.
NEW CTOR
(ai [<agent>] [<heuristics>] [trainedHeuristics:<heuristics>] [<features>] [trainedFeatures:<features>] [trainedFeatureTrees:<featureTrees>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<agent>]: Can be used to specify the agent that is expected to perform best in this game. This algorithm will be used when the ``Ludii AI" option is selected in the Ludii app.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<heuristics>]: Heuristics to be used by Alpha-Beta agents. These may be handcrafted heuristics.
PARAM JAVADOC: [trainedHeuristics:<heuristics>]: Heuristics trained or otherwise generated by some sort of automated process. Alpha-Beta agents will only use these if the previous parameter (for potentially handcrafted heuristics) is not used.
PARAM JAVADOC: [<features>]: Feature sets (possibly handcrafted) to be used for biasing MCTS-based agents. If not specified, Biased MCTS will not be available as an AI for this game in Ludii.
PARAM JAVADOC: [trainedFeatures:<features>]: Automatically-trained feature sets. Will be used instead of the regular ``features'' parameter if that one is left unspecified.
PARAM JAVADOC: [trainedFeatureTrees:<featureTrees>]: Automatically-trained decision trees of features. Will be used instead of the regular ``features'' or ``trainedFeatures'' parameters if those are left unspecified.
EXAMPLE: (ai (bestAgent "UCT"))
REMARKS: Specifying AI metadata for games is not mandatory.
TYPE: metadata.ai.agents.Agent
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes an agent (either by name of expected best agent, or as a   complete setup).
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.agents.BestAgent
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.agents.mcts.Mcts
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.agents.minimax.AlphaBeta
TYPE: metadata.ai.agents.BestAgent
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes the name of an algorithm or agent that is typically expected to  be the best-performing algorithm available in Ludii for this game.
NEW CTOR
(bestAgent <string>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the (expected) best agent for this game.
EXAMPLE: (bestAgent "UCT")
REMARKS: Some examples of names that Ludii can currently recognise are ``Random'', ``Flat MC'', ``Alpha-Beta'', ``UCT'', ``MC-GRAVE'', and ``Biased MCTS''.

TYPE: metadata.ai.agents.mcts.selection.Ag0

(ag0 [<float>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<float>]: The value to use for the exploration constant [2.5].

TYPE: metadata.ai.agents.mcts.selection.Ucb1
