NEW CTOR
(ucb1 [<float>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<float>]: The value to use for the exploration constant [square root of 2].
EXAMPLE: (ucb1)
EXAMPLE: (ucb1 0.6)
TYPE: metadata.ai.agents.minimax.AlphaBeta
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes an Alpha-Beta search agent.
NEW CTOR
(alphaBeta [<heuristics>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<heuristics>]: The heuristics to be used by this agent. Will default to heuristics from the game file's metadata if left unspecified [null].
EXAMPLE: (alphaBeta)
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.FeatureSet
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a single feature set, which may be applicable to either a  single specific player in a game, or to all players in a game.
NEW CTOR
(featureSet <roleType> {<pair>})
PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The Player (P1, P2, etc.) for which the feature set should apply, or All if it is applicable to all players in a game.
PARAM JAVADOC: {<pair>}: Complete list of all features and weights for this feature set.
EXAMPLE: (featureSet All { (pair "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[-{}]>" 1.0) })
EXAMPLE: (featureSet P1 { (pair "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[-{}]>" 1.0) })
NEW CTOR
(featureSet <roleType> [selectionFeatures:{<pair>}] [playoutFeatures:{<pair>}] [tspgFeatures:{<pair>}])
PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The Player (P1, P2, etc.) for which the feature set should apply, or All if it is applicable to all players in a game.
PARAM JAVADOC: [selectionFeatures:{<pair>}]: Complete list of all features and weights for this feature set, for MCTS Selection phase.
PARAM JAVADOC: [playoutFeatures:{<pair>}]: Complete list of all features and weights for this feature set, for MCTS Playout phase.
PARAM JAVADOC: [tspgFeatures:{<pair>}]: Complete list of all features and weights for this feature set, trained with Tree Search Policy Gradients objective.
EXAMPLE: (featureSet P1 selectionFeatures:{ (pair "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[-{}]>" 1.0) } playoutFeatures:{ (pair "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[-{}]>" 2.0) })
REMARKS: Use \All for feature sets that are applicable to all players in a game, or \P1, \P2, etc. for feature sets that are applicable only to individual players.
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.Features
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes one or more sets of features (local, geometric patterns) to be used by Biased MCTS agents.
NEW CTOR
(features [<featureSet>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<featureSet>]: A single feature set.
EXAMPLE: (features (featureSet All { (pair "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<refl=true,rots=all,els=[-{}]>" 1.0) }))
NEW CTOR
(features [{<featureSet>}])
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<featureSet>}]: A sequence of multiple feature sets (typically each applying to a different player).
EXAMPLE: (features { (featureSet P1 { (pair "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[-{}]>" 1.0) }) (featureSet P2 { (pair "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[-{}]>" -1.0) }) })
REMARKS: The basic format of these features is described in: Browne, C., Soemers, D. J. N. J., and Piette, E. (2019). ``Strategic features for general games.'' In Proceedings of the 2nd Workshop on Knowledge Extraction from Games (KEG) (pp. 7075).
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.trees.FeatureTrees
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes one or more sets of features (local, geometric patterns),   represented as decision / regression trees.
NEW CTOR
(featureTrees [logitTrees:{<logitTree>}] [decisionTrees:{<decisionTree>}])
PARAM JAVADOC: [logitTrees:{<logitTree>}]: One or more logit trees (each for the All role or for a specific player).
PARAM JAVADOC: [decisionTrees:{<decisionTree>}]: One or more decision trees (each for the All role or for a specific player).
EXAMPLE: (featureTrees logitTrees:{ (logitTree P1 (if "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[f{0}]>" then:(leaf { (pair "Intercept" 1.0) }) else:(leaf { (pair "Intercept" -1.0) }))) })
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.trees.classifiers.BinaryLeaf
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes a leaf node in a binary classification tree for features; it contains  only a predicted probability for "top move".
NEW CTOR
(binaryLeaf <float>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <float>: Predicted probability of being a top move.
EXAMPLE: (binaryLeaf 0.6)
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.trees.classifiers.DecisionTree
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes a Decision Tree for features (a decision tree representation of a feature set,  which outputs class predictions).
NEW CTOR
(decisionTree <roleType> <decisionTreeNode>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The Player (P1, P2, etc.) for which the logit tree should apply, or All if it is applicable to all players in a game.
PARAM JAVADOC: <decisionTreeNode>: The root node of the tree.
EXAMPLE: (decisionTree P1 (if "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[f{0}]>" then:(leaf bottom25:0.0 iqr:0.2 top25:0.8) else:(leaf bottom25:0.6 iqr:0.35 top25:0.05)))
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.trees.classifiers.DecisionTreeNode
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes a node in a decision tree for features. May either be a condition  node (internal node), or a node with class predictions (leaf node).
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.features.trees.classifiers.BinaryLeaf
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.features.trees.classifiers.If
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.features.trees.classifiers.Leaf
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.trees.classifiers.If
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes a decision node in a decision tree for features; it contains one  feature (the condition we check), and two branches; one for the case  where the condition is true, and one for the case where the condition is false.
NEW CTOR
(if <string> then:<decisionTreeNode> Else:<decisionTreeNode>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The feature to evaluate (the condition).
PARAM JAVADOC: then:<decisionTreeNode>: The branch to take if the feature is active.
PARAM JAVADOC: Else:<decisionTreeNode>: The branch to take if the feature is not active.
EXAMPLE: (if "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[f{0}]>" then:(leaf bottom25:0.0 iqr:0.2 top25:0.8) else:(leaf bottom25:0.6 iqr:0.35 top25:0.05))
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.trees.classifiers.Leaf
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes a leaf node in a binary classification tree for features; it contains  only a predicted probability for "best move".
NEW CTOR
(leaf bottom25:<float> iqr:<float> top25:<float>)
PARAM JAVADOC: bottom25:<float>: Predicted probability of being a bottom-25% move.
PARAM JAVADOC: iqr:<float>: Predicted probability of being a move in the Interquartile Range.
PARAM JAVADOC: top25:<float>: Predicted probability of being a top-25% move.
EXAMPLE: (leaf bottom25:0.0 iqr:0.2 top25:0.8)
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.trees.logits.If
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes a decision node in a logit tree for features; it contains one  feature (the condition we check), and two branches; one for the case  where the condition is true, and one for the case where the condition is false.
NEW CTOR
(if <string> then:<logitNode> Else:<logitNode>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The feature to evaluate (the condition).
PARAM JAVADOC: then:<logitNode>: The branch to take if the feature is active.
PARAM JAVADOC: Else:<logitNode>: The branch to take if the feature is not active.
EXAMPLE: (if "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[f{0}]>" then:(leaf { (pair "Intercept" 1.0) }) else:(leaf { (pair "Intercept" -1.0) }))
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.trees.logits.Leaf
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes a leaf node in a logit tree for features; it contains an array  of features and weights, describing a linear function to use to compute the  logit in this node. An intercept feature should collect all the weights  inferred from features evaluated in decision nodes leading up to this leaf.
NEW CTOR
(leaf {<pair>})
PARAM JAVADOC: {<pair>}: List of remaining features to evaluate and their weights.
EXAMPLE: (leaf { (pair "Intercept" 1.0) })
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.trees.logits.LogitNode
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes a node in a logit tree for features. May either be a condition  node (internal node), or a node with a linear model (a leaf node).
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.features.trees.logits.If
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.features.trees.logits.Leaf
TYPE: metadata.ai.features.trees.logits.LogitTree
TYPE JAVADOC: Describes a Logit Tree for features (a regression tree representation of a feature set,  which outputs logits).
NEW CTOR
(logitTree <roleType> <logitNode>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <roleType>: The Player (P1, P2, etc.) for which the logit tree should apply, or All if it is applicable to all players in a game.
PARAM JAVADOC: <logitNode>: The root node of the tree.
EXAMPLE: (logitTree P1 (if "rel:to=<{}>:pat=<els=[f{0}]>" then:(leaf { (pair "Intercept" 1.0) }) else:(leaf { (pair "Intercept" -1.0) })))
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.Heuristics
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a collection of heuristics, which can be used by Alpha-Beta agent in  Ludii for their heuristics state evaluations.
NEW CTOR
(heuristics [<heuristicTerm>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<heuristicTerm>]: A single heuristic term.
EXAMPLE: (heuristics (score))
NEW CTOR
(heuristics [{<heuristicTerm>}])
PARAM JAVADOC: [{<heuristicTerm>}]: A sequence of multiple heuristic terms, which will all be linearly combined based on their weights.
EXAMPLE: (heuristics { (material) (mobilitySimple weight:0.01) })
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.CentreProximity
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a heuristic term based on the proximity of pieces to the centre of  a game's board.
NEW CTOR
(centreProximity [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] [weight:<float>] [pieceWeights:{<pair>}])
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: [weight:<float>]: The weight for this term in a linear combination of multiple terms. If not specified, a default weight of $1.0$ is used.
PARAM JAVADOC: [pieceWeights:{<pair>}]: Weights for different piece types. If no piece weights are specified at all, all piece types are given an equal weight of $1.0$. If piece weights are only specified for some piece types, all other piece types get a weight of $0$.
EXAMPLE: (centreProximity pieceWeights:{ (pair "Queen" 1.0) (pair "King" -1.0) })
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.ComponentValues
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a heuristic term based on the values of sites that contain  components owned by a player.
NEW CTOR
(componentValues [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] [weight:<float>] [pieceWeights:{<pair>}] [boardOnly:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: [weight:<float>]: The weight for this term in a linear combination of multiple terms. If not specified, a default weight of $1.0$ is used.
PARAM JAVADOC: [pieceWeights:{<pair>}]: Weights for different piece types. If no piece weights are specified at all, all piece types are given an equal weight of $1.0$. If piece weights are only specified for some piece types, all other piece types get a weight of $0$. These weights are multiplied with the values on sites where these pieces are present.
PARAM JAVADOC: [boardOnly:<boolean>]: If true, only pieces that are on the game's main board are counted, and pieces that are, for instance, in players' hands are excluded. False by default.
EXAMPLE: (componentValues boardOnly:True)
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.CornerProximity
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a heuristic term based on the proximity of pieces to the corners of  a game's board.
NEW CTOR
(cornerProximity [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] [weight:<float>] [pieceWeights:{<pair>}])
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: [weight:<float>]: The weight for this term in a linear combination of multiple terms. If not specified, a default weight of $1.0$ is used.
PARAM JAVADOC: [pieceWeights:{<pair>}]: Weights for different piece types. If no piece weights are specified at all, all piece types are given an equal weight of $1.0$. If piece weights are only specified for some piece types, all other piece types get a weight of $0$.
EXAMPLE: (cornerProximity pieceWeights:{ (pair "Queen" -1.0) (pair "King" 1.0) })
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.CurrentMoverHeuristic
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a heuristic term that adds its weight only for the player  whose turn it is in any given game state.
NEW CTOR
(currentMoverHeuristic [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] [weight:<float>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: [weight:<float>]: The weight for this term in a linear combination of multiple terms. If not specified, a default weight of $1.0$ is used.
EXAMPLE: (currentMoverHeuristic weight:1.0)
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.HeuristicTerm
TYPE JAVADOC: Abstract class for heuristic terms. Every heuristic term is expected to implement  a function that outputs a score for a given game state and player, and every term  has a weight that is used for computing linear combinations of multiple terms.
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.CentreProximity
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.ComponentValues
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.CornerProximity
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.CurrentMoverHeuristic
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.Influence
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.InfluenceAdvanced
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.Intercept
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.LineCompletionHeuristic
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.Material
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.MobilityAdvanced
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.MobilitySimple
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.NullHeuristic
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.OwnRegionsCount
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.PlayerRegionsProximity
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.PlayerSiteMapCount
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.RegionProximity
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.Score
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.SidesProximity
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.UnthreatenedMaterial
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.Influence
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a heuristic term that multiplies its weight by the number  of moves with distinct "to" positions that a player has in a current game state,  divided by the number of playable positions that exist in the game.
NEW CTOR
(influence [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] [weight:<float>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: [weight:<float>]: The weight for this term in a linear combination of multiple terms. If not specified, a default weight of $1.0$ is used.
EXAMPLE: (influence weight:0.5)
REMARKS: Always produces a score of $0$ for players who are not the current mover.
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.InfluenceAdvanced
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a heuristic term that multiplies its weight by the number  of moves with distinct "to" positions that a player has in a current game state,  divided by the number of playable positions that exist in the game.  In comparison to Influence, this is a more advanced version that will also attempt  to gain non-zero estimates of the influence of players other than the current  player to move.
NEW CTOR
(influenceAdvanced [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] [weight:<float>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: [weight:<float>]: The weight for this term in a linear combination of multiple terms. If not specified, a default weight of $1.0$ is used.
EXAMPLE: (influenceAdvanced weight:0.5)
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.Intercept
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines an intercept term for heuristic-based value functions, with one  weight per player.
NEW CTOR
(intercept [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] playerWeights:{<pair>})
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: playerWeights:{<pair>}: Weights for different players. Players for which no weights are specified are given a weight of 0.0. Player names must be one of the following: "P1", "P2", ..., "P16".
EXAMPLE: (intercept playerWeights:{ (pair "P1" 1.0) (pair "P2" 0.5) })
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.LineCompletionHeuristic
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a heuristic state value based on a player's potential to  complete lines up to a given target length.  This mostly follows the description of the N-in-a-Row advisor as  described on pages 82-84 of:  	``Browne, C.B. (2009) Automatic generation and evaluation of recombination games.   	PhD thesis, Queensland University of Technology''.
NEW CTOR
(lineCompletionHeuristic [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] [weight:<float>] [targetLength:int])
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: [weight:<float>]: The weight for this term in a linear combination of multiple terms. If not specified, a default weight of $1.0$ is used.
PARAM JAVADOC: [targetLength:int]: The target length for line completions. If not specified, we automatically determine a target length based on properties of the game rules or board.
EXAMPLE: (lineCompletionHeuristic targetLength:3)
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.Material
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a heuristic term based on the material that a player has on  the board and in their hand.
NEW CTOR
(material [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] [weight:<float>] [pieceWeights:{<pair>}] [boardOnly:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: [weight:<float>]: The weight for this term in a linear combination of multiple terms. If not specified, a default weight of $1.0$ is used.
PARAM JAVADOC: [pieceWeights:{<pair>}]: Weights for different piece types. If no piece weights are specified at all, all piece types are given an equal weight of $1.0$. If piece weights are only specified for some piece types, all other piece types get a weight of $0$.
PARAM JAVADOC: [boardOnly:<boolean>]: If true, only pieces that are on the game's main board are counted, and pieces that are, for instance, in players' hands are excluded. False by default.
EXAMPLE: (material pieceWeights:{ (pair "Pawn" 1.0) (pair "Bishop" 3.0) })
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.MobilityAdvanced
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a more advanced Mobility heuristic that attempts to also compute  non-zero mobility values for players other than the current mover (by  modifying the game state temporarily such that it thinks the current mover  is any other player).
NEW CTOR
(mobilityAdvanced [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] [weight:<float>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: [weight:<float>]: The weight for this term in a linear combination of multiple terms. If not specified, a default weight of $1.0$ is used.
EXAMPLE: (mobilityAdvanced weight:0.5)
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.MobilitySimple
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a simple heuristic term that multiplies its weight by the number  of moves that a player has in a current game state.
NEW CTOR
(mobilitySimple [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>] [weight:<float>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [transformation:<heuristicTransformation>]: An optional transformation to be applied to any raw heuristic score outputs.
PARAM JAVADOC: [weight:<float>]: The weight for this term in a linear combination of multiple terms. If not specified, a default weight of $1.0$ is used.
EXAMPLE: (mobilitySimple weight:0.5)
REMARKS: Always produces a score of $0$ for players who are not the current mover.
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.terms.NullHeuristic

(nullHeuristic)
EXAMPLE: (nullHeuristic)

TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.transformations.DivNumBoardSites

NEW CTOR

TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.transformations.DivNumInitPlacement

TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.transformations.HeuristicTransformation
TYPE JAVADOC: Interface for transformations of heuristics (generally functions  intended to map the scores of a heuristic to some different range).
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.transformations.DivNumBoardSites
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.transformations.DivNumInitPlacement
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.transformations.LogisticFunction
SUBCLASS: metadata.ai.heuristics.transformations.Tanh
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.transformations.LogisticFunction
TYPE JAVADOC: Transforms heuristic scores by applying the logistic function to them:  $f(x) = \frac{1}{1 + \exp(x)}$.
NEW CTOR
(logisticFunction)
EXAMPLE: (logisticFunction)
REMARKS: This guarantees that all transformed heuristic scores will lie in $[0, 1]$. May map too many different values only to the limits of this interval in practice.
TYPE: metadata.ai.heuristics.transformations.Tanh
TYPE JAVADOC: Transforms heuristic scores by applying the $\tanh$ to them:  $f(x) = \tanh(x)$.
NEW CTOR
(tanh)
EXAMPLE: (tanh)
REMARKS: This guarantees that all transformed heuristic scores will lie in $[-1, 1]$. May map too many different values only to the limits of this interval in practice.
TYPE: metadata.ai.misc.Pair
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines a pair of a String and a floating point value. Typically used  in AI metadata to assign a numeric value (such as a heuristic score, or  some other weight) to a specific piece name.
NEW CTOR
(pair <string> <float>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The String value.
PARAM JAVADOC: <float>: The floating point value.

TYPE: metadata.graphics.board.Board
TYPE JAVADOC: Sets a graphic data to the board.
NEW CTOR
(board Style <containerStyleType> [replaceComponentsWithFilledCells:<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <containerStyleType>: Container style wanted for the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [replaceComponentsWithFilledCells:<boolean>]: True if cells should be filled instead of component drawn [False].
EXAMPLE: (board Style Chess)
NEW CTOR
(board StyleThickness <boardGraphicsType> <float>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <boardGraphicsType>: The board graphics type to which the colour is to be applied (must be InnerEdge or OuterEdge).
PARAM JAVADOC: <float>: The assigned thickness scale for the specified boardGraphicsType.
EXAMPLE: (board StyleThickness OuterEdges 2.0)
NEW CTOR
(board Checkered [<boolean>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [<boolean>]: Whether the graphic data should be applied or not [True].
EXAMPLE: (board Checkered)
NEW CTOR
(board <pieceGroundType> [image:<string>] [fillColour:<colour>] [edgeColour:<colour>] [scale:<float>] [scaleX:<float>] [scaleY:<float>] [rotation:int] [offsetX:<float>] [offsetY:<float>])
PARAM JAVADOC: <pieceGroundType>: The type of data to apply to the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [image:<string>]: Name of the image to draw. Default value is an outline around the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [fillColour:<colour>]: Colour for the inner sections of the image. Default value is the phase 0 colour of the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [edgeColour:<colour>]: Colour for the edges of the image. Default value is the outer edge colour of the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [scale:<float>]: Scale for the drawn image relative to the size of the board [1.0].
PARAM JAVADOC: [scaleX:<float>]: Scale for the drawn image, relative to the cell size of the container, along x-axis [1.0].
PARAM JAVADOC: [scaleY:<float>]: Scale for the drawn image, relative to the cell size of the container, along y-axis [1.0].
PARAM JAVADOC: [rotation:int]: Rotation of the drawn image (clockwise).
PARAM JAVADOC: [offsetX:<float>]: Offset distance as percentage of board size to push the image to the right [0].
PARAM JAVADOC: [offsetY:<float>]: Offset distance as percentage of board size to push the image to the down [0].
EXAMPLE: (board Background image:"octagon" fillColour:(colour White) edgeColour:(colour White) scale:1.2)
NEW CTOR
(board Colour <boardGraphicsType> <colour>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <boardGraphicsType>: The board graphics type to which the colour is to be applied.
PARAM JAVADOC: <colour>: The assigned colour for the specified boardGraphicsType.
EXAMPLE: (board Colour Phase2 (colour Cyan))
NEW CTOR
(board Placement [scale:<float>] [offsetX:<float>] [offsetY:<float>])
PARAM JAVADOC: [scale:<float>]: scale for the board.
PARAM JAVADOC: [offsetX:<float>]: X offset for board center.
PARAM JAVADOC: [offsetY:<float>]: Y offset for board center.
EXAMPLE: (board Placement scale:0.8)

CONST JAVADOC: Value: To indicates whether the value of a piece should be displayed.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.show.ShowComponentType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the types of Show metadata for a type of components.
CONST JAVADOC: Piece: To indicate that the component to apply the type is a piece.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.show.ShowEdgeType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the types of Draw metadata related to edges.
CONST JAVADOC: Edges: To specify customised drawing of edges in the board graph.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.show.ShowLineType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the types of Draw metadata related to line.
CONST JAVADOC: Line: To draw a specified image on the board.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.show.ShowScoreType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the types of Show metadata for a score.
CONST JAVADOC: Score: To indicate whether the score should be shown only in certain situations.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.show.ShowSiteDataType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the types of Show metadata related to a data of the sites.
CONST JAVADOC: AsHoles: To indicate whether the sites of the board should be represented as holes.
CONST JAVADOC: SiteIndex: Indicates whether the sites of the board should have their index displayed/
TYPE: metadata.graphics.show.ShowSiteType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the types of Show metadata related to a site.
CONST JAVADOC: Sites: To apply it on the sites.
CONST JAVADOC: Cell: To apply it on the cells.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.show.ShowSymbolType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines the types of Draw metadata related to symbol.
CONST JAVADOC: Symbol: To draw a specified image on the board.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.util.BoardGraphicsType
CONST JAVADOC: InnerEdges: Edges that are not along a board side.
CONST JAVADOC: OuterEdges: Edges that define a board side.
CONST JAVADOC: Phase0: Cells in phase 0, e.g. dark cells on the Chess board.
CONST JAVADOC: Phase1: Cells in phase 1, e.g. light cells on the Chess board.
CONST JAVADOC: Phase2: Cells in phase 2, e.g. for hexagonal tiling colouring.
CONST JAVADOC: Phase3: Cells in phase 3, e.g. for exotic tiling colourings.
CONST JAVADOC: Phase4: Cells in phase 4, e.g. for exotic tiling colouring.
CONST JAVADOC: Phase5: Cells in phase 5, e.g. for exotic tiling colourings.
CONST JAVADOC: Symbols: Symbols drawn on the board, e.g. Senet, Hnefatafl, Royal Game of Ur...
CONST JAVADOC: InnerVertices: Intersections of lines on the board, e.g. where Go stones are played.
CONST JAVADOC: OuterVertices: Intersections of lines on the board, along the perimeter of the board.

CONST JAVADOC: ExtendedShogi: Extended style for Shogi pieces.

CONST JAVADOC: NativeAmericanDice: Style for native american dice.

TYPE: metadata.graphics.util.PieceColourType

CONST JAVADOC: Fill: Fill colour.
CONST JAVADOC: Edge: Edge colour.
CONST JAVADOC: Secondary: Secondary colour. Used for things like the count colour.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.util.PieceStackType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines different ways of visualising stacks of pieces.
CONST JAVADOC: Default: Stacked one above the other (with offset).
CONST JAVADOC: Ground: Spread on the ground, e.g. Snakes and Ladders or Pachisi.
CONST JAVADOC: GroundDynamic: Spread on the ground, but position based on size of stack.
CONST JAVADOC: Reverse: Reverse stacking downwards.
CONST JAVADOC: Fan: Spread to show each component like a hand of cards.
CONST JAVADOC: FanAlternating: Spread to show each component like a hand of cards, alternating left and right side of centre.
CONST JAVADOC: None: No visible stacking.
CONST JAVADOC: Backgammon: Stacked Backgammon-style in lines of five.
CONST JAVADOC: Count: Show just top piece, with the stack value as number.
CONST JAVADOC: DefaultAndCount: Stacked one above the other (with offset), with the stack value as number.
CONST JAVADOC: CountColoured: Show just top piece, with the stack value as number(s), coloured by who.
CONST JAVADOC: Ring: Stacked Ring-style around cell perimeter.
CONST JAVADOC: TowardsCenter: Stacked towards the center of the board.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.util.PuzzleDrawHintType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines different ways of visualising stacks of pieces.
CONST JAVADOC: Default: Hints drawn in the middle.
CONST JAVADOC: TopLeft: Hints drawn in the top left.
CONST JAVADOC: NextTo: Draw the hint next to the region.
CONST JAVADOC: None: No hints.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.util.PuzzleHintLocationType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines different ways of visualising stacks of pieces.
CONST JAVADOC: Default: Hints placed on top-left site of region.
CONST JAVADOC: BetweenVertices: Draw hint on edge between vertex.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.util.StackPropertyType
TYPE JAVADOC: Defines different aspects of a stack.
CONST JAVADOC: Scale: Stack scale.
CONST JAVADOC: Limit: Stack maximum number of pieces (used by some stack types).
CONST JAVADOC: Type: Stack design.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.util.ValueLocationType
TYPE JAVADOC: Specified where to draw state of an item in the interface, relative to its position.
CONST JAVADOC: None: No location.
CONST JAVADOC: CornerLeft: At the top left corner of the item's location.
CONST JAVADOC: CornerRight: At the top left corner of the item's location.
CONST JAVADOC: Top: At the top of the item's location.
CONST JAVADOC: Middle: Centred on the item's location.
TYPE: metadata.graphics.util.WhenScoreType
TYPE JAVADOC: Specifies when to show player scores to the user.
CONST JAVADOC: Always: Always show player scores.
CONST JAVADOC: Never: Never show player scores.
CONST JAVADOC: AtEnd: Only show player scores at end of game.

PARAM JAVADOC: int: Green component [0..255].

(colour int int int int)
PARAM JAVADOC: int: Red component [0..255].
PARAM JAVADOC: int: Green component [0..255].
PARAM JAVADOC: int: Blue component [0..255].
PARAM JAVADOC: int: Alpha component [0..255].
EXAMPLE: (colour 255 0 0 127)

(colour <string>)

EXAMPLE: (colour "#00ff1a")

(colour <userColourType>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <userColourType>: Predefined user colour type.

TYPE: metadata.info.database.Aliases
TYPE JAVADOC: Specifies a list of additional aliases for the game's name.
NEW CTOR
(aliases {<string>})
PARAM JAVADOC: {<string>}: Set of additional aliases for the name of this game.
EXAMPLE: (aliases {"Caturanga" "Catur"})
TYPE: metadata.info.database.Author
TYPE JAVADOC: Specifies the author of the game or ruleset.
NEW CTOR
(author <string>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The author of the game.
EXAMPLE: (author "John Doe")
TYPE: metadata.info.database.Classification
TYPE JAVADOC: Specifies the location of this game within the Ludii classification scheme.
NEW CTOR
(classification <string>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The game's location within the Ludii classification scheme.
EXAMPLE: (classification "games/board/war/chess")
REMARKS: The Ludii classification is a combination of the schemes used in H. J. R. Murray's {\it A History of Board Games other than Chess} and David Parlett's {\it The Oxford History of Board Games}, with additional categories to reflect the wider range of games supported by Ludii.
TYPE: metadata.info.database.Credit
TYPE JAVADOC: Specifies the author of the .lud file and any relevant credit information.
NEW CTOR
(credit <string>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The author of the .lud file.
EXAMPLE: (credit "A. Fool, April Fool Games, 1/4/2020")
REMARKS: The is *not* for the author of the game or ruleset. The "author" info item should be used for that.
TYPE: metadata.info.database.Date
TYPE JAVADOC: Specifies the (approximate) date that the game was created.
NEW CTOR
(date <string>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The date the game was created.
EXAMPLE: (date "2015-10-05")
REMARKS: Date is specified in the format (YYYY-MM-DD).

TYPE: metadata.info.database.Version
TYPE JAVADOC: Specifies the latest Ludii version that this .lud is known to work for.
NEW CTOR
(version <string>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: Ludii version in String form.
EXAMPLE: (version "1.0.0")
REMARKS: The version format is (Major version).(Minor version).(Build number). For example, the first major version for public release is "1.0.0".
TYPE: metadata.recon.ReconItem
TYPE JAVADOC: Metadata containing some specific reconstruction requirements.
SUBCLASS: metadata.recon.concept.Concept
TYPE: metadata.recon.concept.Concept
TYPE JAVADOC: Specifies the what concept values are required.
NEW CTOR
(concept <string> (<float>  | <boolean>))
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the concept.
PARAM JAVADOC: <float>: The double value.
PARAM JAVADOC: <boolean>: The boolean value.
EXAMPLE: (concept "Num Players" 6)
NEW CTOR
(concept <string> minValue:<float> maxValue:<float>)
PARAM JAVADOC: <string>: The name of the concept.
PARAM JAVADOC: minValue:<float>: The minimum value.
PARAM JAVADOC: maxValue:<float>: The maximum value.
EXAMPLE: (concept "Num Players" minValue:2 maxValue:4)
DEFINE: IsInCheck
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a specific piece is threatened by any other enemy piece. #1 = The name of the piece (without the number). #2 = The roleType of the owner of the piece. #3 = The location where is the piece or The specific moves used to threat. This parameter is optional. If not specify the current location of the piece is used and all the legal moves are used. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsInCheck" "Osho" Next)
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsInCheck" "King" Mover at:(to))
DEFINE: IsEnemyAt
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if an enemy is on a site. #1 = The site. #2 = The level [the topest]. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsEnemyAt" (to))
DEFINE: IsFriendAt
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a friend is on a site. #1 = The site. #2 = The level [the topest]. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsFriendAt" (to))
DEFINE: AllOwnedPiecesIn
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if all pieces on the board owned by the mover are in a region. #1 = The region. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("AllOwnedPiecesIn" (sites Top))
DEFINE: DieNotUsed
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a die is not used when using the ludeme (forEach Die ...). 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("DieNotUsed")
DEFINE: HandEmpty
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if all the sites in a specific hand are empty. This ludemeplex is working only for non stacking games. #1 = The owner of the hand, can be a RoleType or the index of the owner. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("HandEmpty" Mover)
DEFINE: HandOccupied
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if at least a site in a specific hand is not empty. This ludemeplex is working only for non stacking games. #1 = The owner of the hand, can be a RoleType or the index of the owner. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("HandOccupied" Mover)
DEFINE: HasFreedom
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a group of pieces has some liberties around it. The specified directions (by default Adjacent) are the directions between the elements of the group. #1 = = Directions of the pieces in the group. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("HasFreedom" Orthogonal)
DEFINE: IsEmptyAndNotVisited
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a site is empty and not visited so far in the same turn. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsEmptyAndNotVisited" (to))
DEFINE: IsPhaseOne
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a site is phase 1. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsPhaseOne" (between))
DEFINE: IsPhaseZero
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a site is phase 0. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsPhaseZero" (between))
DEFINE: IsPieceAt
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a piece #1 owned by #2 is at a site #3. #1 = The name of the piece. #2 = The owner of the piece. #3 = The site. #4 = The level. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsPieceAt" "Ball" Shared 32)
DEFINE: IsSingleGroup
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if only one single group with pieces owned by a player exists. #1 = The owner of the pieces in the group. #2 = The direction used to connect the pieces in the group (by default Adjacent). 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsSingleGroup" Mover)
DEFINE: NoPieceOnBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if the board is empty. This ludemeplex is not working for games involving stacks. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("NoPieceOnBoard)
DEFINE: NoSites
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a region has no sites. #1 = The region. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("NoSites" (sites Empty))
DEFINE: IsEmptyOrSingletonStack
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a stack has a size of 1 at a site or if the site is empty. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsEmptyOrSingletonStack" (to))
DEFINE: IsSingletonStack
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a stack has a size of 1 at a site. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsSingletonStack" (to))
DEFINE: IsTopLevel
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a level is at the top of a stack. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsTopLevel" (to))
DEFINE: NoEnemyOrOnlyOne
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if no enemy or only one in a stack game. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("NoEnemyOrOnlyOne" (to))
DEFINE: IsEndTrack
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a site returned by a track is the ending site of the track. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsEndTrack" ("NextSiteOnTrack" 3))
DEFINE: IsNotEndTrack
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a site returned by a track is not the ending site of the track. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsNotEndTrack" ("NextSiteOnTrack" 3))
DEFINE: IsNotOffBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a site returned by a track is not off board. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsNotOffBoard" ("NextSiteOnTrack" 3))
DEFINE: IsOffBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if a site returned by a track is off board. #1 = The site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("IsOffBoard" ("NextSiteOnTrack" 3))
DEFINE: NewTurn
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if this is new turn, i.e. the current move is not the previous mover. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("NewTurn")
DEFINE: SameTurn
DEFINE JAVADOC: Checks if the previous mover is the same player than the current mover, consequently this is the same turn. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("SameTurn")
DEFINE: LastDirection
DEFINE JAVADOC: Returns the direction between the last `from' location and the last `to' location. #1 = The site type of the sites. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("LastDirection" Cell)
DEFINE: DraughtsEquipment
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines all the equipment used in most of the draught games. #1 = The graph of the board. #2 = The default site type to use [Optional by default Cell]. #3 = An optional element of the equipment. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("DraughtsEquipment" (square 8))
DEFINE: CrossBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a regular start board (example: Kaooa). #1 = The dimension of the start. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("StarBoard" 5)
DEFINE: LascaBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines the original Lasca board. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("LascaBoard")
DEFINE: StarBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a regular cross board tilled by squares (example: Pachisi). #1 = The dimension of an arm of the cross. #2 = The full dimension of the board. #3 = The default site type of the board. #4 = The type of the diagonals of each tiling. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("CrossBoard" 3 7 use:Vertex diagonals:Alternating)
DEFINE: AlquerqueBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a rectangular board with Alquerque-style alternating diagonals. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("AlquerqueBoard" 5 5)
DEFINE: AlquerqueBoardWithBottomAndTopTriangles
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a rectangular board with Alquerque-style alternating diagonals with a triangle extension at the bottom and another at the top. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("AlquerqueBoardWithBottomAndTopTriangles")
DEFINE: AlquerqueBoardWithBottomTriangle
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a rectangular board with Alquerque-style alternating diagonals with a triangle extension at the bottom. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("AlquerqueBoardWithBottomTriangle")
DEFINE: AlquerqueBoardWithEightTriangles
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a rectangular board with Alquerque-style alternating diagonals with eight triangle extensions. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("AlquerqueBoardWithEightTriangles")
DEFINE: AlquerqueBoardWithFourTriangles
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a rectangular board with Alquerque-style alternating diagonals with four triangle extensions on each side. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("AlquerqueBoardWithFourTriangles")
DEFINE: NineMensMorrisBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a nine men's morris board. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("NineMensMorrisBoard")
DEFINE: ThreeMensMorrisBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a Three Men's Morris board. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("ThreeMensMorrisBoard")
DEFINE: ThreeMensMorrisBoardWithLeftAndRightTriangles
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a Three Men's Morris board with two triangle extensions at the left and right. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("ThreeMensMorrisBoardWithLeftAndRightTriangles")
DEFINE: BackgammonBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a backgammon board (without the style). #1 = The tracks of the players. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("BackgammonBoard")
DEFINE: FortyStonesWithFourGapsBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a circle board defined with 40 stones, with a gap after each 10 stones. The board is playable on the edges. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("FortyStonesWithFourGapsBoard")
DEFINE: KintsBoard
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a rectangular board with some arcs used in some native american games such as Kints. #1 = The tracks of the players.

DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a step move to all the rotational directions to an empty site. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("StepRotationalToEmpty")
DEFINE: StepStackToEmpty
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a step move of a full stack to all the directions specified (adjacent by default) to an empty site. #1 = The direction(s) to step. #2 = The consequences. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("StepStackToEmpty")
DEFINE: StepToEmpty
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a step move to all the directions specified (adjacent by default) to an empty site. #1 = The direction(s) to step. #2 = The consequences. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("StepToEmpty")
DEFINE: StepToEnemy
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a step move to all the directions specified (adjacent by default) to a site occupied by an enemy piece. The enemy piece is removed. #1 = The direction(s) to step. #2 = The consequences. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("StepToEnemy")
DEFINE: StepToNotFriend
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a step move to all the directions specified (adjacent by default) to a site occupied by an enemy piece or an empty site. The enemy piece is removed. #1 = The direction(s) to step. #2 = The consequences. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("StepToNotFriend")
DEFINE: BeforeAfterCentreSetup
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines starting rules placing one piece on each site before and after the centre (e.g. Starting rules of Zamma). #1 = The name of the piece of P1. #2 = The name of the piece of P2. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("BeforeAfterCentreSetup" "Marker1" "Marker2")
DEFINE: BlackCellsSetup
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines starting rules placing one counter on each black cell of a square board (e.g. Starting rules of Draughts). #1 = The number of rows to place pieces for each player. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("BlackCellsSetup" 3)
DEFINE: BottomTopSetup
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines starting rules placing one piece on each cell of the bottom and the top rows of the board (e.g. Starting rules of Breakthrough). #1 = The number of rows to place pieces for each player. #2 = The name of the piece of P1. #3 = The name of the piece of P2. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("BottomTopSetup" 3 "Counter1" "Counter2")
DEFINE: WhiteCellsSetup
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines starting rules placing one counter on each white cell of a square board (e.g. Starting rules of Draughts). #1 = The number of rows to place pieces for each player. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("WhiteCellsSetup" 3)
DEFINE: DominoWalk
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a graphics turtle walk to build a domino as a large piece. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("DominoWalk")
DEFINE: GiraffeWalk
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a graphics turtle walk to get the locations where can move a Chess giraffe. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("GiraffeWalk")
DEFINE: KnightWalk
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a graphics turtle walk to get the locations where can move a Chess knight. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("KnightWalk")
DEFINE: LWalk
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a graphics turtle walk to build a large L piece. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("LWalk")
DEFINE: TWalk
DEFINE JAVADOC: Defines a graphics turtle walk to build a large T piece. 
DEFINE EXAMPLE: ("TWalk")
